features and bug fixes","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-update-mac","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac683198669500182b5876?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Apple MacBook event 2020\" height=\"906\" width=\"1812\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>It should only take a few clicks to update your Mac.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Apple</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li><strong>To update your Mac, open the System Preferences app, which has its own \"Software Update\" menu.</strong></li>\n<li>You can also check for updates through the \"About This Mac\" menu, which can be found by clicking the Apple logo in the top-left corner of your screen.</li>\n<li><strong>If your Mac is still running macOS High Sierra or earlier, however, you'll need to go through the App Store.</strong></li>\n<li><strong>With the new macOS Big Sur release, you should update your Mac as soon as you can.</strong></li>\n<li><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tech-reference\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"summary_bullets\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"0\">Visit Business Insider's Tech Reference library for more stories</a>.</strong></li>\n</ul><p>In many ways, <a style=\"font-family: Georgia, Times, sans-serif;\" href=\"http://bestbuy.7tiv.net/c/196318/614286/10014?subId1=bi_051419_how-to-update-mac&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bestbuy.com%2Fsite%2Fapple-macbook-pro-13-display-with-touch-bar-intel-core-i5-8gb-memory-128gb-ssd-latest-model-space-gray%2F5998700.p%3FskuId%3D59987008700\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Macs</a> are built for convenience: They have backlit keyboards, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/where-do-screenshots-go-on-mac\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">there's a variety of ways to take and save screenshots</a>, and they come with a wide assortment of shortcuts that can speed up your work.</p><p>But like all devices, they also require updates from time to time. And although updates can be annoying and time-consuming — Who hasn't put off an update until the very last moment? — they're also incredibly important.</p><p>An outdated Mac is more susceptible to bugs, crashes, and even viruses (yes, Macs can get them too). And if you leave updates waiting for too long, your favorite apps might stop working altogether.</p><p>In November 2020, Apple released macOS Big Sur, the latest version of its famous operating system. And if you're currently working on a Mac, now is a good time to update your computer.&#160;</p><h2><strong style=\"color: #000000;\">How to update your Mac computer</strong></h2><p>There are two major ways to update your Mac, and which one you use will depend on what macOS version you're currently running. For information on how to check which macOS version you currently have, read our article, \"<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-check-mac-os-version\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">How to check which version of macOS your Mac computer is running and check for new updates</a>.\"</p><p>Before going forward with updates, it's a good idea to <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-backup-mac\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">backup your computer</a> to ensure no data is lost in the process. You'll also need to be connected to the internet.</p><p>After that, keep in mind that the updates may take several minutes to install, depending on how many of your apps are due for updates.</p><h3>How to update a Mac running macOS Mojave or later</h3><p>If you've bought or updated your Mac since 2018, chances are that you're in this category.</p><p><strong>1.&#160;</strong>In the top-right corner of your screen, click the Apple icon to open a drop-down menu.</p><p><strong>2.&#160;</strong>There are two menus here that you can use to check for updates. Click either \"System Preferences\" or \"About This Mac...\"</p><p><strong>3.</strong> No matter which one you pick, in the menu that opens, click \"Software Update.\"</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac66f47f8f4200182a668b?format=jpeg\" alt=\"how to update mac 2\" height=\"931\" width=\"1106\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>There are multiple ways to reach the updating screen.\n<p class=\"copyright\">William Antonelli/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>3.&#160;</strong>Wait a few moments for your Mac to connect to the internet and check for updates. If an update is available, you'll be shown what it's called — just click \"Update Now\" to install it.</p><p>You can also choose to enable automatic updates from this screen by checking the \"Automatically keep my Mac up to date\" box. This will ensure that whenever a new update is available, you'll be told without having to open this screen.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5da5f15a4af909531c18f9b2?format=jpeg\" alt=\"software_update\" height=\"464\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Click &#34;Update Now&#34; to update, and check the box pictured to enable automatic updates.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Apple; Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><h3>How to update a Mac running macOS High Sierra or earlier</h3><p>High Sierra was released in late 2017. If you haven't updated since then, you should be sure to update as soon as you can to keep your computer safe.</p><p><strong>1. </strong>Click the Apple icon in the top-left corner of your screen.</p><p><strong>2. </strong>Select \"App Store…\"</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5cd9dc15021b4c4022197b88?format=jpeg\" alt=\"SCREENSHOT UPDATE MAC 1\" height=\"586\" width=\"871\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Open the App Store.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Devon Delfino/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>3. </strong>Click \"Updates\" in the left sidebar of the App Store.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5cd9dc3d021b4c4bfe1e99d6?format=jpeg\" alt=\"SCREENSHOT UPDATE MAC 2\" height=\"732\" width=\"1191\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Navigate to the Updates page.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Devon Delfino/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>From the above screen, you'll be given the option to update your Mac. Any Mac computer released in 2012 or later should be able to update to at least macOS Catalina.&#160;If your Mac is so old that it can't even do that, it might be time to buy a new model.</p><p>And, for future reference, don't worry about accepting an update and then having your computer unexpectedly restart —&#160;you'll be notified beforehand if a restart is required.</p><div On the downside, some owners mention that the glass lids break easily and that the metal discolors after use at high heat. This is a common issue with most stainless steel that is not fully clad with aluminum, however.</p>\n\tThe best starter set\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5dfbd7c3855cc206e8181db4?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Vremi cookware\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>The inexpensive <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B017JDY3LM/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_012518_best-cookware-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B017JDY3LM&#38;linkId=0c08c33cd0fca30c9a3875a8fcddd421\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Vremi 15-Piece Nonstick Cookware Set</a> is an ideal starter set for someone who is starting out in their first apartment.</h3><p><strong>Pros</strong>: Colorful, bargain price, nonstick and easy to clean, good heat conductivity</p><p><strong>Cons</strong>: Small pots and pans, some complaints of handles coming loose, some complaints of discoloration after use</p><p>If you're looking for an affordable cookware starter pack, check out the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B017JDY3LM/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_012518_best-cookware-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B017JDY3LM&#38;linkId=0c08c33cd0fca30c9a3875a8fcddd421\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow sponsored\">Vremi 15-Piece Nonstick Cookware Set</a>. The 8-inch and 10-inch frying pans, 1-quart, 1.5-quart, and 2-quart saucepans with lids, and the 5-quart Dutch oven feature enamel layered over an aluminum core that conducts heat evenly and effectively.</p><p>You also get a five-piece set of non-scratch cooking utensils that includes a masher, slotted spoon, ladle, turner, and pasta server.</p><p>Admittedly, you aren't going to get the finest quality for such a bargain price, but this is still a decent set of cookware that performs quite well. The nonstick coating is easy to clean, the glass lids fit well, and the set performs nicely on low-to-medium heat. You can even pop the pots or pans into the oven up to 480 degrees.</p><p>Overall, this is a great choice for someone looking to stock their first kitchen, or someone who only cooks occasionally.</p><p>Some owners complain the handles come loose too easily and the pots and pans are all small sizes, but those are the only negatives.</p><p>&#160;</p>\n\tThe best cast iron\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5a6a17fc1784251f008b487a?format=jpeg\" alt=\"lodge cookware\" height=\"654\" width=\"872\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Lodge</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>For searing meat to the perfect brown, transfer easily from stovetop to oven, and last practically forever, you'll appreciate the <a href=\"https://go.skimresources.com?id=35871X943606&#38;xs=1&#38;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.campingworld.com%2Flodge-5-piece-cast-iron-set-236012.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Lodge 5-Piece Cast Iron Set</a>.&#160;</h3><p><strong>Pros</strong>: The Dutch oven's lid also fits the larger skillet, incredibly durable, holds heat longer than any other type of cookware, pre-seasoned</p><p><strong>Cons</strong>: If you don't like the weight or maintenance of cast iron, this isn't the set for you</p><p>There's a certain mystique to cooking with cast iron. Yes, it can be a pain to clean and season &#8211; although the <a href=\"https://go.skimresources.com?id=35871X943606&#38;xs=1&#38;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.campingworld.com%2Flodge-5-piece-cast-iron-set-236012.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Lodge Logic 5-Piece Cast Iron Set</a>&#160;is pre-seasoned to take care of that chore for you &#8211; and yes, it is very heavy, which can be a con for those with arthritis or weak arms. But it's hard to beat cast iron when it comes to searing a steak, baking stovetop cornbread, or scrambling eggs.</p><p>While you won't find saucepans or stockpots made of cast iron, you will find skillets and Dutch ovens. And Lodge brings both together in its five-piece set that includes a 5-quart Dutch oven with lid, an 8- and 10-inch skillet, and a 10-inch griddle.</p><p>With proper care, you can pass your Lodge cookware set down to your children, and they can pass it on to your grandchildren. But while you're still using the cookware, you'll enjoy the foundry-seasoned, naturally nonstick interiors, the integral handles &#8211; no wiggling or loose handles here &#8211; and the way the pieces can cook over any type of heat. They can handle induction, gas, electric, oven, grill, and even an open campfire.</p><h3><a href=\"http://www.businessinsider.com/best-cast-iron-skillet\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Raed our full buying guide to the best cast iron skillets and pans</a></h3>\n\tThe best splurge\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5a6a26aacf84100d018b47a4?format=jpeg\" alt=\"All-Clad cookware\" height=\"600\" width=\"800\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">All-Clad</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>The <a href=\"https://click.linksynergy.com/deeplink?id=EHFxW6yx8Uo&#38;mid=13867&#38;u1=biipgf_012518_best-cookware&#38;murl=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bloomingdales.com%2Fshop%2Fproduct%2Fall-clad-d5-stainless-brushed-10-piece-cookware-set%3FID%3D1074049%26pla_country%3DUS%26CAWELAID%3D120156070001414532%26CAGPSPN%3Dpla%26CAAGID%3D47685649199%26CATCI%3Dpla-383392021161%26cm_mmc%3DGoogle-PLA-ADC-_-Desktop_Non_RLSA_Non_Trade-_-home-_-11644896683USA%26gclid%3DEAIaIQobChMI09n4-Yiu5QIVpoNaBR3AigTqEAQYAyABEgJr0fD_BwE\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow sponsored\">All-Clad d5 Stainless Steel 10-Piece Cookware Set</a> brings professional-level quality to the home kitchen.</h3><p><strong>Pros</strong>: Finest quality stainless steel cookware clad with multiple layers of aluminum for superior heat conductivity, limited lifetime warranty, stick-resistant surface, riveted heat-resistant handles</p><p><strong>Cons</strong>: Very expensive</p><p>All-Clad has a well-deserved reputation for manufacturing some of the finest pots and pans available. Its cookware sets also have a reputation for being quite expensive. But as they say, you get what you pay for, so if you are able and willing to splurge, the <a href=\"https://click.linksynergy.com/deeplink?id=EHFxW6yx8Uo&#38;mid=13867&#38;u1=biipgf_012518_best-cookware&#38;murl=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bloomingdales.com%2Fshop%2Fproduct%2Fall-clad-d5-stainless-brushed-10-piece-cookware-set%3FID%3D1074049%26pla_country%3DUS%26CAWELAID%3D120156070001414532%26CAGPSPN%3Dpla%26CAAGID%3D47685649199%26CATCI%3Dpla-383392021161%26cm_mmc%3DGoogle-PLA-ADC-_-Desktop_Non_RLSA_Non_Trade-_-home-_-11644896683USA%26gclid%3DEAIaIQobChMI09n4-Yiu5QIVpoNaBR3AigTqEAQYAyABEgJr0fD_BwE\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow sponsored\">All-Clad d5 Stainless Steel 10-Piece Cookware Set</a> will bring superb quality to your kitchen.</p><p>The 10-piece set includes 8- and 10-inch skillets, 2- and 4-quart covered saucepans, a 4-quart saut&#233; pan with lid, and an 8-quart covered stockpot. All are made with 5-ply bonded construction that alternates layers of stainless steel and aluminum for the utmost in heat conductivity, meaning the pots and pans heat slowly and evenly to perfectly brown and cook your food.</p><p>The cookware is safe for oven and broiler up to 600 degrees and is also suitable for induction cooking.</p>\n\tTypes of pots and pans\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5835c8b1ba6eb67d058b5f6f?format=jpeg\" alt=\"pots pans rachael ray\" height=\"1125\" width=\"1500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<ul style=\"list-style-type: disc; padding-left: 30px; font-family: Georgia,Times,sans-serif;\"><li><strong>Skillet</strong>: Also called a frying pan, a skillet is a kitchen workhorse used for frying, saut&#233;ing, grilling, searing, and browning foods. Skillets have gently sloping, shallow sides, a wide bottom, a long handle, and often, no lid. Frying pans are measured by the size across the top of the pan. The most common sizes are 8-inch, which is perfect for a grilled cheese sandwich or scrambled eggs for one, 10-inch, which is perfect for everyday use if you are only cooking for one or two people, and 12-inch, which is good if you are cooking for a family.</li><li><strong style=\"color: #222222;\">Saut&#233; pan</strong>: A saut&#233; pan is similar to a skillet, and the terms are sometimes used interchangeably. A saut&#233; pan has straight sides (skillets have gently sloped sides), a long handle, and sometimes a smaller loop handle on the other side for ease in lifting the pan. Most saut&#233; pans include a lid. Use your saut&#233; pan to saut&#233;, braise, or cook up any large batch of food with a lot of liquid. A 5-quart saut&#233; pan is the most useful size or 3-quart if you only cook for one or two people.</li><li><strong style=\"color: #222222;\">Saucepan</strong>: The pot you will reach for over and over, saucepans are round, with straight sides, a long handle, and a fitted lid. Saucepans are perfect for heating and cooking soups, stews, rice, sauces, or vegetables. Saucepans are measured in quarts. A 2-quart and a 4-quart saucepan will cover your needs nicely.</li><li><strong style=\"color: #222222;\">Stockpot</strong>: A tall, round pot with a fitted lid, stockpots are perfect for large batches of soups or stews, corn on the cob, or pasta. Stockpots are measured in quarts and an 8-quart pot is large enough to handle a family's needs.</li></ul>\n\tWhich metal is best for cookware?\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5a5fc7ccf421496e3d8b5376?format=jpeg\" alt=\"cookware\" height=\"1125\" width=\"1500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Anolon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<ul style=\"list-style-type: disc; padding-left: 30px; font-family: Georgia,Times,sans-serif;\"><li><strong>Stainless steel</strong> is one of the most popular materials for cookware sets, and for good reason. It doesn't react with foods, works with just about every cooking technique, is very durable and resistant to scratches, dents, and rust, and is safe for the dishwasher (although it's best to wash your cookware by hand). Stainless steel does not conduct heat well, however, so you'll usually find it reinforced with either aluminum or copper. Most stainless steel works with induction cooktops.</li><li><strong style=\"color: #222222;\">Aluminum</strong> is very soft on its own, so almost all cookware made of this reasonably priced metal is <a href=\"http://www.businessinsider.com/best-cookware-hard-anodized/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">anodized</a> &#8211; a process that hardens and strengthens the aluminum, and also reduces its tendency to react with acidic foods like tomatoes. Aluminum is a great conductor of heat and is suitable for most cooking methods. It resists scratches and stains and is easy to care for. Aluminum cookware is usually not compatible with induction cooktops.</li><li><strong style=\"color: #222222;\">Nonstick</strong> pots and pans are generally anodized aluminum coated with a nonstick material, such as Teflon, that prevents food from sticking. This makes cleanup a breeze, particularly with sticky foods such as cheese. On the downside, the nonstick coating tends to scratch easily and wear away over time. You'll need to be careful while stirring or mixing; use plastic or silicone utensils to avoid scratching the cookware. Nonstick pots and pans are generally not safe for very high heat, and although they are dishwasher safe, doing so can speed up the disintegration of the nonstick coating. Most nonstick cookware is not suitable for induction cooktops.</li><li><strong>C</strong><strong style=\"color: #222222;\">opper</strong> is hard to beat for warm natural beauty, but you'll pay a premium for cookware made from this super-conductive metal. Copper reacts to changes in temperature very quickly, meaning it will heat up and cool down faster than most other cookware metals, thus giving you close control over your favorite dishes. On the downside, because copper is reactive, it usually has to be lined with another metal, such as stainless steel, and it requires polishing to maintain its glow. It's also prone to scratches and discoloration, and it's not compatible with induction cooktops.</li><li><strong style=\"color: #222222;\">Carbon steel</strong> is something like a hybrid of cast iron and stainless steel, but much more expensive than either of those metals. It's lighter than cast iron, heats up faster and conducts heat better than cast iron, and develops a natural, somewhat nonstick surface just like cast iron. It also requires periodic seasoning, rusts easily, and reacts with some foods &#8211; also traits of cast iron. Despite its flaws, many chefs love the tight temperature control carbon steel offers, as it responds quickly to changes in the heat. It's also suitable for use with an induction cooktop.</li><li><strong>C</strong><strong style=\"color: #222222;\">ast iron&#160;</strong>cookware sets are rare, but it's a very popular metal for skillets, saucepans, and Dutch ovens. This heavy metal is actually not a good conductor of heat, but once it heats up, it stays hot for a long time. <a href=\"http://www.businessinsider.com/best-cast-iron-skillet\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Cast iron</a> is great for searing meats, scrambling eggs, and baking cornbread, and it goes into the oven just as easily as it cooks on top of it. It requires periodic seasoning, however, is very prone to rust and discoloring, and can be a pain to clean, although it does develop a naturally nonstick surface. Enameled cast iron is a little easier to care for, but is very expensive. Cast iron is suitable for induction cooktops.</li></ul>\n\tMore great cookware guides\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5ede50f6f34d056b9d31cba6?format=jpeg\" alt=\"pots and pans\" height=\"600\" width=\"800\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://www.flickr.com/photos/clothpaperstring/1480817907/\" target=\"_blank\">Flickr / sarah</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<ul class=\"summary-list\"><li><a href=\"http://www.businessinsider.com/best-cookware-hard-anodized/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">The best hard anodized cookware sets</a></li><li><a href=\"http://www.businessinsider.com/best-cast-iron-skillet\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">The best cast iron skillets and pans</a></li></ul>\n</div><div Vrbo","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-vacation-rentals-outer-banks","description":"<p class=\"financial-disclaimer\"><i>When you buy through our links, we may earn money from our affiliate partners. <a href=\"https://www.insider-inc.com/commerce-on-insider-inc/\">Learn more.</a></i></p><p><a href=\"https://airbnb.pvxt.net/c/196318/264339/4273?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.airbnb.com%2Frooms%2F29483737%3Fsource_impression_id%3Dp3_1594665391_opFeyInZ4%252FGzU8Ie%26guests%3D1%26adults%3D1\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\"><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f0caa281918240aa110ffc7?format=jpeg\" alt=\"best vacation rentals outer banks\" height=\"800\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Airbnb</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></a></p><ul class=\"summary-list\"><li><strong>The Outer Banks is a 130-mile-long string of barrier islands off the coast of North Carolina, easily reachable by car.&#160;</strong></li><li><strong>Dotted with quaint beach towns, sleepy fishing villages, and 75 miles of protected coastline, the Outer Banks is ideal for travelers looking to book a private home and practice social distancing.</strong></li><li><strong>We selected highly-rated vacation homes across the Outer Banks on <a href=\"https://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/6415797/type/dlg/https://www.vrbo.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Vrbo</a> and <a href=\"https://airbnb.pvxt.net/c/196318/264339/4273?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.airbnb.com%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Airbnb</a> that range from $90 to $242 per night to start.</strong></li><li><strong>Read more:&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/are-airbnbs-safe-coronavirus\" data-analytics-module=\"summary_bullets\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"20\">Are Airbnbs safe? We spoke to experts, a company representative, and an Airbnb host to share everything you should know before booking someone's home</a>.</strong></li></ul><p>When the hit Netflix series \"Outer Banks\" debuted in April 2020, it introduced many people to this string of barrier islands off the coast of North Carolina.</p><p>But I've known about them for decades, having vacationed every year in the Outer Banks — often shortened to OBX — since I was a teenager. This once low-key destination has since boomed in popularity thanks to wide, white-sand beaches, relatively affordable rental homes, and proximity to many large East Coast cities. Ramshackle single-story beach cottages have given way to sprawling, multi-level houses and fancy restaurants, gourmet stores, and kitschy shops have all moved in.&#160;</p><p>Yet even with this explosive growth — and the persistent snarl of summer traffic — the Outer Banks still manages to retain its natural beauty and charm. The centrally-located beach towns of Kitty Hawk, Nags Head, and Kill Devil Hills tend to be more crowded, but offer family-friendly amenities, while if you head farther north to Corolla, or south to Hatteras, you'll be rewarded with miles of pristine beaches, rugged dunes, lighthouses, and the occasional wild horse.</p><p>As people continue to look for safe travel options where outdoor activities are plentiful amid the ongoing pandemic, all that coastal scenery and space make the Outer Banks especially appealing. Not to mention even the winter temperatures stay in the high 50s and low 60s. when Of course, safety cannot be guaranteed without a vaccine, and it's important to follow guidelines from the CDC and WHO, consider your own risk, and confirm rules mandated by states for visitors. Additionally, follow safety tactics such as washing your hands, wearing a mask, and practicing social distancing.</p><p>However, it's reassuring to know that <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/are-airbnbs-safe-coronavirus\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"20\">experts and the CDC consider renting a vacation home to be one of the safer options</a>, especially <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/which-is-safer-airbnb-hotels-coronavirus\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"20\">compared to hotels</a>. <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/airbnb-vrbo-homeaway\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Airbnb and Vrbo homes</a> are primarily private accommodations, which lowers the potential risks and many offer contactless check-in and are implementing stringent new cleaning measures.</p><p>The <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/airbnb-new-cleaning-protocol\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"20\">Airbnb Enhanced Clean</a> was developed with medical and hospitality experts and includes upgraded cleaning standards for all hosts.&#160;</p><p>Vrbo has implemented enhanced cleaning guidelines for its owners, and guests can use a search filter to view homes that have been \"Highly Rated for Cleanliness,\" and those that have been awarded a \"Cleanliness Rating\" badge for the highest cleanliness reviews. <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/what-is-vrbo\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Here's a handy guide</a> understanding the differences between the platforms so you can decide which is best for you.&#160;</p><p>In the Outer Banks, you'll find everything from cozy vintage cottages to massive new-builds on both Airbnb and Vrbo.</p><p><strong>We selected top homes from each platform based on the following criteria:</strong></p><ol><li>Listings are for the entire home, cottage, or stand-alone apartment to avoid interaction with owners or other guests, in line with recommended COVID-19 precautions.</li><li>Each property is priced between $90 and $242 per night to start, depending on the season.</li><li>All are top-rated Airbnb and Vrbo listings located throughout the Outer Banks with a review score of 4.6 or higher.</li><li>Each property has a variety of appealing amenities including private pools, hot tubs, and decks with water views, and many are within walking distance of the beach.&#160;</li></ol><p>While nightly rates start under $258, these are average prices, and rates fluctuate by the season. Rentals near the beach are generally more expensive and homes often come with minimum stays and cleaning and service fees, which are not included in nightly rates. Finally, some amenities or facilities may be closed as a result of COVID, so be sure to contact the host for more information prior to booking.&#160;</p><h2>These are the best vacation rentals in the Outer Banks on Airbnb and Vrbo, sorted by price from low to high.</h2>\n<div id=\"slideshow\">\n\tA secluded stay in Kitty Hawk, $90\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f0cad1df34d0517eb098919?format=jpeg\" alt=\"4375d49a 87f2 48ec 89a1 ebd74b755a82.f10\" height=\"768\" width=\"1024\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Vrbo</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h2><a href=\"https://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/6415797/type/dlg/https://www.vrbo.com/1601302?adultsCount=1\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Book this cottage starting at $90 per night on Vrbo</a></h2><p>Much of the Kitty Hawk rental market is focused on beach access, which means houses are often packed closely together, on small lots, and with little privacy. 12:49:39","updatedTime":"2020-11-12 12:49:39","title":"You can't sign out of your Epic Games account on your PS4 directly, but you can unlink your accounts from the Epic Games website — here's how","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-sign-out-of-epic-games-account-on-ps4","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fa9b35cf7d1cb0019e3aa7e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"man playing video games with controller on couch\" height=\"1249\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>You can essentially log out of an Epic Games account on a PS4 by unlinking Epic Games from your PlayStation Network account.\n<p class=\"copyright\">simonkr/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>You can't directly sign out of your Epic Games account on PS4, but you can effectively sign out by unlinking your Epic Games account from your PlayStation Network account.&#160;</li>\n<li>To sign out of your Epic Games account on your PS4, you need to disconnect your accounts from the Epic Games website.&#160;</li>\n<li><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tech-reference\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"summary_bullets\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"0\">Visit Business Insider's Tech Reference library for more stories</a>.</strong></li>\n</ul><p>If you want to sign out of your <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/category/epic-games\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Epic Games</a> account that's linked to your <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/category/playstation-network\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">PlayStation Network</a> account, you might feel perplexed at how to do so.&#160;</p><p>The <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/category/ps4\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">PS4</a> doesn't currently have an application that allows you to sign in and out of your Epic Games account. Fortunately, there's a workaround you can try from the Epic Games website.</p><h2><strong>How to sign out of Epic Games account on PS4</strong></h2><p>Because the Epic Games app isn't compatible with your PS4 directly, you'll have to go to the Epic Games website to sign out.</p><p><strong>1.</strong> Go to the <a href=\"https://www.epicgames.com/store/en-US/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Epic Games website</a> on your computer, and log in to your account.</p><p><strong>2.</strong> Hover your cursor over your username in the upper right corner of the screen so that a dropdown menu appears. In the dropdown menu, click \"Account.\"&#160;</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fa98f5d1df1d50018219a35?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How_to_link_Epic_Games_account_to_PS4_ _2\" height=\"827\" width=\"1841\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Click &#34;Account&#34; in the dropdown menu under your username.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Chrissy Montelli/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>3.</strong> In the sidebar, click on \"Connections.\"&#160;</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fa9900cf7d1cb0019e3a963?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How_to_link_Epic_Games_account_to_PS4_ _3\" height=\"817\" width=\"1791\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Click &#34;Connections&#34; from the menu on the left.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Chrissy Montelli/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>4.</strong> Click the \"Accounts\" tab.&#160;</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fa99073f7d1cb0019e3a967?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How_to_link_Epic_Games_account_to_PS4_ _4\" height=\"822\" width=\"1748\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Click on &#34;Accounts.&#34;\n<p class=\"copyright\">Chrissy Montelli/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>5.</strong> Scroll down to the Playstation Network field and click the gray \"Disconnect\" button.&#160;</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fa9af07f7d1cb0019e3aa5d?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How_to_sign_out_of_Epic_Games_account_on_PS4_ _4\" height=\"800\" width=\"1764\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Click &#34;Disconnect&#34; in the tile for PlayStation Network.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Chrissy Montelli/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>6.</strong> A pop-up window will appear. To sign out of your Epic Games account, you must click each of the boxes in the pop-up window. Once all the boxes are checked, click \"Unlink.\"&#160;</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fa9afcc1df1d50018219b32?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How_to_sign_out_of_Epic_Games_account_on_PS4_ _5\" height=\"839\" width=\"1700\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Check all the boxes and click &#34;Unlink.&#34;\n<p class=\"copyright\">Chrissy Montelli/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Your Epic Games account should now be signed out on your PS4.</p><div id=\"ProductCard_5d9f8c02cc4a0a07897870b2\" style=\"position:relative; display:block; width: 100%\"><iframe 6/cdn83@2020_6/2020/11/12/04-50-04-632_7a9b2af71ff1f48c.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1605156579260},{"createdTime":"2020-11-12 12:49:39","updatedTime":"2020-11-12 12:49:39","title":"Trump campaign witness says it's 'odd' that US troops voted for Biden in large numbers","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/military-veteran-vote-joe-biden-trump-lawsuit-2020-11","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac7a1d98669500182b58ad?format=jpeg\" alt=\"joe biden korea\" height=\"1500\" width=\"3000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Then Vice President Joe Biden with South Korean and US soldiers inside the Demilitarized Zone on December 7, 2013.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Lee Jin-man/Pool via AP</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>President Trump's 2020 reelection campaign on Wednesday filed a lawsuit against the state of Michigan, alleging the ballot-handling and -counting process had disenfranchised voters.</li>\n<li>Attorneys for the campaign attached to their lawsuit dozens of notarized statements from Michigan voters, Republican poll watchers, and other observers to corroborate Trump's claims &#8212; including one who merely said it was strange that many US service members voted for President-elect Joe Biden.</li>\n<li>\"I had always been told that military personnel tended to be more conservative, so this stuck out to me as the day went on,\" the observer said in his statement.</li>\n<li>Recent polling showed US troops had a high disapproval rating for Trump and were split over which candidate they would vote for.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>President Donald Trump's 2020 reelection campaign on Wednesday filed a <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trump-michigan-election-lawsuit-poll-watchers-social-distancing-complaints-2020-11\">lawsuit</a> against the state of Michigan, alleging the ballot-handling and -counting process had disenfranchised voters through \"fraud and incompetence.\"</p><p>Attorneys for the campaign attached to their lawsuit dozens of notarized statements from Michigan voters, Republican poll watchers, and other observers to corroborate Trump's claims — including one who said it was peculiar that droves of US service members voted for President-elect Joe Biden.</p><p>\"I did find it odd that, throughout the day/night, I saw a few dozen military ballots be counted,\" a certified poll watcher said in his statement dated November 4. \"Although I cannot provide specific numbers or names, I can estimate that at least 80% of the military ballots I saw were straight ticket Democrat or simply had Joe Biden's name filled in on them.\"</p><p>\"I had always been told that military personnel tended to be more conservative, so this stuck out to me as the day went on,\" he added.</p><p>The poll watcher, who was stationed at the TCF convention center in Detroit and said he had a \"GOP network of friends,\" also alleged he faced intimidation by his colleagues after scrutinizing their actions and calling for a ballot review. He was eventually escorted out of the location by police officers after debating with a supervisor.</p><p>The layout of absentee ballots vary by state, and some designs make it easier to tell if they are from a US service member. Overseas Michigan residents, such as service members, are allowed to vote through an electronic ballot that may be mailed in the event that physical ballots are not available — on top of these ballots are the words \"MILITARY AND OVERSEAS VOTER BALLOT,\" according to a Michigan Bureau of Elections manual dated March 2018.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac660f98669500182b5868?format=jpeg\" alt=\"poll watcher\" height=\"2000\" width=\"3000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>An observer watches as county employees process mail-in ballots in Las Vegas on October 31.\n<p class=\"copyright\">John Locher/AP</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>But the poll observer's anecdote of seeing an overwhelmingly majority of \"military\" ballots at his location supporting Democrats is being met with some pushback, particularly in the wake of Trump's declining approval rating in recent polls and his attitude toward some veterans.</p><p>According to a poll from the <a href=\"https://www.militarytimes.com/news/pentagon-congress/2020/08/31/as-trumps-popularity-slips-in-latest-military-times-poll-more-troops-say-theyll-vote-for-biden/\">Military Times and Syracuse University's Institute for Veterans and Military Families</a> conducted in July, 42% of 1,018 active-duty military respondents said they strongly disapproved of Trump's tenure at the White House. Nearly half of the poll's respondents said they viewed Trump unfavorably. That poll showed Biden with a 4-percentage-point lead over Trump.</p><p>But a separate <a href=\"https://morningconsult.com/2020/09/10/2020-military-voters-trump-biden-polling/\">Morning Consult</a> poll found Trump with a 10-percentage-point lead over Biden from military-affiliated households in October.&#160;</p><p>Despite Trump's professed love toward US service members and veterans, several reports published this year have thrown that rosy assessment into doubt. In September, <a href=\"https://www.theatlantic.com/politics/archive/2020/09/trump-americans-who-died-at-war-are-losers-and-suckers/615997/\">The Atlantic</a>&#160;published a scathing report that said Trump disparaged dead military veterans.</p><p>The report, written by Editor in Chief Jeffrey Goldberg, cited officials who said they heard Trump describing Marines who died during World War I as \"losers\" and \"suckers\" and that he did not want injured veterans to appear at a military parade because he believed it would make spectators uneasy.</p><p>Trump's opinion of the late Republican Sen. John McCain, a longtime Arizona lawmaker and US Navy veteran, also incensed veterans' groups and congressional leaders with military service. After McCain died from an aggressive form of brain cancer in 2018, Trump was angry when the senator received half-staff flag honors, The Atlantic reported. Trump was outspoken about his negative assessment of McCain and previously rejected the notion of describing him as a war hero \"because he was captured\" during the Vietnam War.</p><p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/military-vets-against-trumps-army-polls-election-2020-11\">Common Defense</a>, a nonprofit organization seeking to elect progressive candidates, questioned the long-standing belief that military service members and veterans would be inclined to support Republican candidates.</p><p>\"The current military is as diverse as the population we are drawn from and serve,\" a Common Defense spokesman told Insider. \"And if there is one thing that unifies us, no matter where we fall on the political spectrum, it is our frustration with the perception that we are the props for any particular politician or political party.\"</p><p>The spokesman added: \"Common Defense has campaigned for four years to mobilize veterans in swing states like Michigan to vote against Donald Trump, and so it is no surprise to us that military ballots in Detroit favored President-elect Joe Biden.\"</p><p>Trump's allies have relied on anecdotal evidence, such as the poll observer's claim in Michigan, and set up hotlines offering rewards to those who can corroborate their allegations of voter fraud. For instance, Texas Republican Lt. Gov. Dan Patrick this week offered $1 million of his own money for evidence of voter fraud.</p><p>So far, the Trump campaign's lawsuits in numerous battleground states have lacked evidence. According to a <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/2020/11/10/us/politics/voting-fraud.html\">New York Times</a> report published Tuesday, election officials from 45 states said they witnessed no evidence of fraud or major issues with voting. Insider's Grace Panetta previously <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/voter-election-fraud-statistics-rare-president-biden-trump-2020-2020-11\">reported</a> an \"American is more likely to be struck by lightning than to commit election fraud,\" citing a dataset of past convictions.</p><p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/2020-election-results\">Insider and Decision Desk HQ</a> have projected that Biden won Michigan's 16 Electoral College votes.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a border=\"0\"></img></a>\n</div><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/GSi9u_X0gFc\" height=\"1\" width=\"1\" alt=\"\"/>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Wed, 11 Nov 2020 23:44:07 +0000","feedId":22,"bgimg":"https://i.insider.com/5fac7a0a7f8f4200182a66cd?format=jpeg","linkMd5":"23a03dfb0c0dd06950cfd874695271f4","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx25/cdn20@2020_3/2020/11/12/04-49-56-222_e235e9f73786078b.webp","destWidth":2160,"destHeight":1620,"sourceBytes":140278,"destBytes":140278,"author":"dchoi@businessinsider.com (David Choi)","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://i.insider.com/5fac7a1d98669500182b58ad?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn84@2020_1/2020/11/12/04-49-59-308_2c577aaa6b41168c.webp","https://i.insider.com/5fac660f98669500182b5868?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx2/cdn67@2020_6/2020/11/12/04-50-00-900_66ed2e8e19621de3.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn11@2020_1/2020/11/12/04-50-05-069_cc3ef43fc8ff5801.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=GSi9u_X0gFc:eO_CdPZ93ws:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx3/cdn32@2020_5/2020/11/12/04-49-58-557_12382e32002e500f.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=GSi9u_X0gFc:eO_CdPZ93ws:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx31/cdn75@2020_2/2020/11/12/04-49-56-219_e736c721abb35d60.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn48@2020_5/2020/11/12/04-49-59-767_740defb435ea442b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=GSi9u_X0gFc:eO_CdPZ93ws:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn56@2020_4/2020/11/12/04-50-06-572_c518cbd98a3ca2c8.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/GSi9u_X0gFc":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn75@2020_5/2020/11/12/04-50-06-508_48a9cbc81f627cb8.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1605156579242},{"createdTime":"2020-11-12 12:49:39","updatedTime":"2020-11-12 12:49:39","title":"'We need more help': El Paso's Republican mayor says the city needs a second stimulus to protect public health","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/el-paso-mayor-dee-margo-discusses-surge-in-covid-19-2020-11","description":"<figure> \n <img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac95ee4044a00018f7617e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"GettyImages 1229386967\" height=\"1250\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\"> \n  <figcaption>\n   EL PASO, TX - OCTOBER 31: Cars pass through a coronavirus testing site at the University of Texas El Paso on October 31, 2020 in El Paso, Texas. As El Paso reports record numbers of active coronavirus cases, the Texas Attorney General sues to block local shutdown orders. \n   <p class=\"copyright\">Cengiz Yar/Getty Images</p> \n  </figcaption> </img>\n</figure>\n<ul class=\"summary-list\"> \n <li>El Paso Mayor Dee Margo told Business Insider he's struggling \"walk that tight wire\" between public health and ensuring small businesses don't go under during the pandemic.</li> \n <li>At least 26,000 people in El Paso currently have COVID-19, with over 1,000 in the hospital.</li> \n <li>Margo, a Republican, was an early proponent of masks but has been hesitant to shut down non-essential businesses during the latest surge.</li> \n <li>\"I recognize that there are physical deaths as a result of this pandemic, and physical hurt with families and others,\" Margo said. \"But there also are financial deaths that are occurring.\"</li> \n <li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li> \n</ul>\n<p>Dee Margo is the mayor of a city in crisis. Over 26,000 people in El Paso, a border city of some 680,000 in Texas, currently have COVID-19, a thousand of them are in the hospital. Fourteen people were reported dead on Wednesday alone, 696 since the pandemic began. The surge in fatalities is outstripping the city's ability to store the bodies; it now has 10 mobile morgues — air-conditioned trucks — to prevent corpses from decaying.</p>\n<p>\"I wish I were omnipotent — to be able to know what to do and how to do it,\" Margo, a Republican facing an upcoming runoff election, told Business Insider on Wednesday.</p>\n<p>Unlike some in his party, Margo was an early advocate of masks, pushing back against Texas Gov. Greg Abbott and his since-rescinded prohibition on local mandates. But he does share the reticence to shutter businesses.</p>\n<blockquote class=\"twitter-tweet blockquote\" data-lang=\"en\" data-cards=\"\" data-conversation=\"\">\n —City of El Paso (@ElPasoTXGov) \n <a href=\"https://twitter.com/mims/statuses/1326540604763852802?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw\">November 11, 2020</a>\n</blockquote>\n<script async=\"\" src=\"//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"></script>\n<p>Last month, an El Paso County judge, Ricardo Samaniego attempted to <a href=\"https://apnews.com/article/virus-outbreak-texas-el-paso-prisons-2c8c536c178dd7464740876e64352fd7\">force such closures</a>, issuing a two-week shutdown order for all non-essential businesses, from gyms to tattoo parlors, and limit restaurants to take-out and delivery. Samaniego extended that order Wednesday.</p>\n<p>Margo's administration at first declined to enforce the order, which faces an ongoing legal challenge from a group of El Paso restaurants and the Texas attorney general. Uncertainty reigned, El Paso's restaurants continuing to serve diners and, per the city's contact-tracing program, contributed to the spread of the coronavirus.</p>\n<p>\"Huge, huge confusion,\" Laura Rayborn, a local spa owner, <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/2020/11/10/us/coronavirus-hospitalizations-el-paso-texas.html\">told The New York Times</a>. \"The mayor went on the radio and on TV and said, 'Stay open.\"</p>\n<p>\"We were between a rock and a hard place, legally,\" Margo argued, citing Gov. Abbott's own executive order limiting the ability of local jurisdictions to impose lockdowns. A district court later upheld the judge's order and, on Nov. 6, El Paso police began enforcing it. It is the most stringent set of restrictions since April, when the city lifted a stay-at-home order.<strong><br /></strong></p>\n<p>The law was not Margo's only consideration. He knows that bars — and bars adding food trucks so they can evade the city's public health edicts and stay open as restaurants — contribute to the spread of the coronavirus. Indoor dining, too: in October, Margo limited dining establishments to carry out after 9:00 p.m., reducing the maximum occupancy to 50% before that.</p>\n<p>\"When you drink alcohol, your guard goes down and people drop their protections,\" Margo said. That was the thinking that informed the restrictions. However, \"what we found is that people were leaving the bars after 9:00 p.m., but they weren't going home. They were congregating in other homes together or other locations together.\" Over half of positive COVID-19 cases in El Paso are people between the ages of 20 to 39. \"That's still a behavioral issue that's a problem.\"</p>\n<p>Shopping, too, is to blame for the spread: Contact-tracing has revealed that one of the top apparent sources of infection <a href=\"https://www.ktsm.com/news/big-box-stores-top-source-of-covid-19-spread-in-el-paso-officials-say/\">are big-box retailers</a> — Walmart, Target, and the like — where extended families walk the aisles in search of bargains. <strong><br /></strong></p>\n<p>Ideally, perhaps, these places would be limited to delivery or curbside pickup too. The status quo of doing just enough to arrest the spread of the virus, but not enough to stamp it out, has meant states and cities across the country, red and blue, have seen progress followed by another surge.</p>\n<p>\"I recognize that there are physical deaths as a result of this pandemic, and physical hurt with families and others,\" Margo said. \"But there also are financial deaths that are occurring.\"</p>\n<figure> \n <img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac95ac7f8f4200182a66f2?format=jpeg\" alt=\"GettyImages 1229244828\" height=\"1666\" width=\"2223\" charset=\"\"> \n  <figcaption>\n   A store closing banner hangs above Trump 2020 hats on a storefront on October 23, 2020 in downtown El Paso, Texas. \n   <p class=\"copyright\">PAUL RATJE/AFP via Getty Images</p> \n  </figcaption> </img>\n</figure>\n<p>A quarter of El Paso's small businesses have shut down since March. \"They're not underground. They're not waiting to resurface. They're gone,\" Margo said. \"We have 32,000 under unemployment, and we have 148,000 people being fed by our food bank. So there is a balance to this. And all I've been trying to do is walk that tight wire.\"</p>\n<p>Shutdowns are, to be sure, a last resort — a hammer that's brought down when a virus is out of control. They might not prevent individual bad behavior, or entire families behaving irresponsibly, but they would, at a time when cities are resorting to morgues on wheels, arrest the spread of a deadly virus. In the long run, temporary pain could also mean long-term economic gain, putting an end to the stop-and-start pattern that's now repeating for a third time.</p>\n<p>Provided, of course, that there was a coherent and consistent federal response. No city is an island, and even those with the strictest responses to the pandemic have been unable to stave off a resurgence in the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/covid-19-harvards-dr-thomas-tsai-asseses-trumps-pandemic-response-2020-7\">absence of a coherent federal plan</a>.<strong><br /></strong></p>\n<p>A second stimulus has been stalled in Congress for months. Democrats have been calling for a comprehensive package, including $1,200 checks, money for state and local governments, and billions more in funding for small business loans, and passed such a measure in May. Senate Republicans, however, have balked at the price tag, with Majority Leader Mitch McConnell putting a new stimulus on the backburner while the chamber confirmed Supreme Court Justice Amy Comey Barrett.<strong><br /></strong></p>\n<p>Trump administration, meanwhile, has veered between calls to cut off negotiations on a new stimulus deal and to \"go big\" — too big, even, for conservatives in Congress. <strong><br /></strong></p>\n<p>\"If you had the financial support that we had at the beginning.... then yeah, that's fine. People can still put food on the table and they still can pay their rent and the businesses can get by,\" Margo said. \"But without that, then it's a morality play. And that bothers me.\" Without that financial support — grants for small businesses and stimulus checks for their patrons — the result is that both the economy and public health suffers.</p>\n<p>\"We need more help,\" Margo told Business Insider. \"We continue to need more help.\"</p>\n<p><em>Have a news tip? Email this reporter: <a href=\"mailto:cdavis@insider.com\">cdavis@insider.com</a></em></p>\n<div class=\"read-original\">\n Read the original article on \n <a President Donald Trump and how he can hold power inside the Republican Party despite losing the White House. pages","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-add-links-to-tumblr-bio","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f3d8aaf42f43f001ddfde83?format=jpeg\" alt=\"man using keyboard on laptop computer\" height=\"1867\" width=\"2800\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>It&#39;s easy to add links to your Tumblr bio on a computer.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Westend61/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>To add links to your Tumblr bio, you'll need to use a simple HTML code.</li>\n<li>Tumblr doesn't give you any sort of built-in way to add links yourself, so you'll have to copy and paste the code in manually.</li>\n<li>Adding links to your Tumblr bio is a great way to give visitors access to your other social media accounts, selected works, information page, and more.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tech-reference\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"summary_bullets\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"0\" data-uri=\"4c86c1c3a45644bf07d168dc4c802e5e\">Visit Business Insider's Tech Reference library for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/category/tumblr\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Tumblr</a> is a popular blogging site that lets you share photos, text posts, videos and music with your friends and followers. It's a great place for artists, writers, and other people who want to share their work with others.</p><p>But if you want visitors to have access to your other social media accounts or content off the site, you can include a link in your blog's bio.</p><p>Tumblr doesn't tell you how to add links when you edit your bio, so it's not obvious that you even can. But it's surprisingly simple, as long as you know how to copy and paste.</p><h2><strong>How to add links to your Tumblr bio</strong></h2><p>Including a clickable URL requires some basic coding. To edit your account, you'll want to start at your feed, or Dashboard.&#160;</p><p><strong>1. </strong>Open Tumblr in a web browser and log in, and then head to your dashboard.</p><p><strong>2. </strong>Click the icon in the top-right that looks like a person's head and shoulders.</p><p><strong>3. </strong>Under the blog that you want to edit, click \"Edit appearance.\" If the blog you want doesn't have any options underneath, hover your mouse over its name and click the head-and-shoulders icon that appears next to it.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fa9bce9f7d1cb0019e3aabd?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to delete Tumblr 2\" height=\"1381\" width=\"2560\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Select the &#34;Edit appearance&#34; option.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Vivian McCall/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>4. </strong>On the \"Blog Options\" page that opens, click \"Edit theme.\"</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5faad91ff7d1cb0019e3adf7?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to add links to your Tumblr bio 2\" height=\"1394\" width=\"2560\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Your blog&#39;s bio is part of its &#34;theme.&#34;\n<p class=\"copyright\">Vivian McCall/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>5. </strong>In the left sidebar, click the text underneath \"Description.\" This is your blog's current bio.</p><p><strong>6. </strong>Now it's time to add your link. Copy and paste this code into the description box, in the place where you want your link to be:</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac59dd98669500182b5814?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Screen Shot 2020 11 11 at 4.38.13 PM\" height=\"50\" width=\"249\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>7. </strong>Insert your link in place of \"URL\" and what you want the text to be in place of \"TITLE.\" Remember to delete the quotation marks.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5faadafc1df1d50018219ed9?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to add links to your Tumblr bio 3\" height=\"1443\" width=\"2560\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>If you want multiple links, just use the code multiple times, wherever you want it.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Vivian McCall/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>8. </strong>Hit \"Save\" at the top of the sidebar, and then \"Exit.\"</p><p>Your link should now be active in your Tumblr bio.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5faadb2d1df1d50018219edc?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to add links to your Tumblr bio 4\" height=\"1231\" width=\"1731\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Your link will appear in your bio, exactly as you formatted it.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Vivian McCall/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><h2>Related coverage /cdn4@2020_6/2020/11/12/04-49-56-517_5021a92187523c8e.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1605156579258},{"createdTime":"2020-11-12 12:49:39","updatedTime":"2020-11-12 12:49:39","title":"Deutsche Bank calls for a baby boomer tax to narrow the generational wealth gap with millennials","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/baby-boomer-tax-generational-wealth-gap-deutsche-bank-2020-11","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac2af57f8f4200182a64cf?format=jpeg\" alt=\"baby boomer\" height=\"1666\" width=\"2222\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Deutsche Bank is proposing redistributing wealth from boomers to millennials to close the generational wealth gap.\n<p class=\"copyright\">NurPhoto/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>A new Deutsche Bank Research <a href=\"https://www.dbresearch.com/PROD/RPS_EN-PROD/PROD0000000000513730/Konzept_%23_19%3A_What_we_must_do_to_rebuild.PDF?undefined&realload=zKSDD1JbMMR4LWIUoEuJSoI3V/Io3riOK2Sd4jg8rTkeK8lVkADKuJbnD01ArzJII15t2sDPtIcxz5daPpyxjA==jA==\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"40\" data-uri=\"cca39a2107530f33fbf867f31d0d2ac4\">report</a> suggests taxing baby boomers to help narrow the millennial-boomer generational wealth gap.</li>\n<li>Instead of an age-related tax, the bank urges a focus on five key forces that have created financial gains for boomers: low interest rates, urbanization, pollution, cohort size, and education.</li>\n<li>The bank proposes taxes on primary residences and other assets such as stocks and bonds as boomers sell them into retirement to avoid higher income taxes.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>The <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/millennials-net-worth-versus-baby-boomers-generational-wealth-gap-2019-8\">generational wealth gap</a> is stark.</p><p>Multiple reports comparing millennials' wealth and earnings to that of boomers when they were millennials' age in the 1980s tell the story: Millennials hold four times less US wealth than boomers held, according to <a href=\"https://www.federalreserve.gov/releases/z1/dataviz/dfa/distribute/table/#quarter:119;series:Net%20worth;demographic:generation;population:all;units:shares\">Fed data</a>, while a <a href=\"https://www.magnifymoney.com/blog/banking/net-worth-of-millenials/\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\" data-uri=\"5c2aba577905c164b0f6a0e2e65dedb3\">MagnifyMoney study</a> found a $600,000 gap between the generations' average net worths at the same age. And a <a href=\"https://www.newamerica.org/millennials/reports/emerging-millennial-wealth-gap/\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\" data-uri=\"a8a103af50e87c93ea79838e96ee6b3f\">report by think tank New America</a> revealed that millennials earn 20% less than boomers did.</p><p>A new Deutsche Bank Research <a href=\"https://www.dbresearch.com/PROD/RPS_EN-PROD/PROD0000000000513730/Konzept_%23_19%3A_What_we_must_do_to_rebuild.PDF?undefined&realload=zKSDD1JbMMR4LWIUoEuJSoI3V/Io3riOK2Sd4jg8rTkeK8lVkADKuJbnD01ArzJII15t2sDPtIcxz5daPpyxjA==jA==\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"40\" data-uri=\"cca39a2107530f33fbf867f31d0d2ac4\">report</a> is suggesting a tax on baby boomers to help narrow this millennial-boomer financial disparity. \"Younger generations have been hit particularly hard while older folk have reaped the benefits,\" it reads, calling for a redistribution of wealth from the old to the young.</p><p>But the report argues against an age-related tax, acknowledging that many boomers worked hard to earn their wealth. Instead, it urges a focus on five key areas where boomers reaped financial gains through luck and external forces: low interest rates, urbanization, pollution, cohort size, and education.</p><p>Boomers, the report says, have benefited from an increased value in assets thanks to low-interest rates and from inflated housing prices. They didn't have to pay as much for education as millennials currently do, nor will they have to face the cost for environmental damage caused by the carbon emission-releasing companies in which they've invested. The generation is also larger in size, the report continues, meaning it typically wins elections.</p><p>With these five forces in mind, the report proposes several tax policies to help close the wealth divide:</p><ul><li><strong>Tax on primary residence</strong> via tax on the profit of the house sale (a capital gains tax) or tax on the property purchase (a stamp duty tax) to offset inflated housing prices</li><li><strong>Additional taxes on financial assets</strong> such as stocks and bonds to offset growth from low-interest rates as boomers begin to sell these assets into retirement</li><li><strong>A \"super tax\" on stocks</strong> to compensate for gains companies made on pollution, which could help fund investment in climate change&#160;</li></ul><p>These taxes, the report states, are intended to avoid higher income taxes. \"These can be an invasion on hard work and, should they rise, there is a risk that work will be disincentivised,\" it reads.</p><p>The report also calls for policies apart from taxation, such as lowering housing prices or centralizing control of city planning, which it recognized as a \"dramatic step\" to leveling the effects of urbanization. For the rising cost of education, the report suggests government subsidies for higher education or government grants to new graduates for the first few working years that will compensate for entry-level salaries less than tuition costs. More powerful youth advisory councils may also address the bigger challenge of imbalance in generational size, the report adds.</p><p>The report notes that some of these policies are more realistic, others more radical, and some may overlap, rendering others unnecessary. But the time for change is now, it says, before millennials take control.&#160;<br><br>\"All indications are that they will enact policies that not only forcibly redistribute in blunt ways, but also upend the<br>very foundations of capitalism,\" the report states.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a presidential election, President Donald Trump appears to be neglecting his duties to govern. He has spent much of the past week falsely alleging voter fraud and then once a winner was projected, refusing to concede to President-elect Joe Biden.</p><p>On Wednesday, Trump visited Arlington National Cemetery for a Veteran's Day ceremony. It was his first appearance in six days, and he did not speak at the event, <a href=\"https://edition.cnn.com/2020/11/11/politics/donald-trump-schedule-election/index.html\">CNN</a> reported.</p><p>White House deputy press secretary Judd Deere told CNN that Trump is \"carrying out all of his duties.\"</p><p>\"Just as he promised, President Trump is fighting hard for a free and fair election while at the same time carrying out all of his duties to put America First,\" Deere said.</p><p>CNN noted that the last intelligence briefing on Trump's public schedule was for October 2, the morning after he tested positive for the coronavirus. While the public schedule does not have all of the president's meetings and events, it has been relatively empty for the past several days.&#160;</p><p>As Trump has stayed out of the public view, the US has been hitting records in new cases of COVID-19 as officials across the country try to figure out how to stop the rapid spread of the virus. On Tuesday, a record of almost 131,000 new cases was recorded and hospitalizations also hit an all-time high.&#160;</p><p>Public health experts have said this could be the \"deadliest\" wave yet, but Trump has not addressed the growing number of cases. deal.&#160;</p><p>Trump had gone after the platform, which is owned by ByteDance, a Chinese-based company for national security concerns.</p><p>The Trump administration <a 12:49:39","updatedTime":"2020-11-12 12:49:39","title":"A short history of US fighter aircraft — from biplanes to stealth jets","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/the-fighter-planes-and-jets-the-us-military-has-used-2020-11","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fa99075f7d1cb0019e3a968?format=jpeg\" alt=\"f 15\" height=\"1050\" width=\"2100\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>F-15C Eagles fly over Okinawa during a solar eclipse.\n<p class=\"copyright\">USAF/Airman 1st Class Chad Warren</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>For the better part of a century, US pilots have fought to control the sky over battlefields all around the world.</li>\n<li>Fighter aircraft have always been at the leading edge of those battles, and the US has fielded some of the most advanced fighters ever built.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>The surest way to secure the skies over a battlefield is with fighter aircraft, and nobody knows that better than the US Air Force.</p><p>Though America's aerial-warfare beginnings were humble, the Air Force now has the world's best fighters.</p><p>With over 100 years of service, Air Force fighter jets have met every challenge they've faced and are constantly evolving in order to control the skies.</p><h2>SPAD XIII</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5faae7aa1df1d50018219fa1?format=jpeg\" alt=\"SPAD XIII fighter plane\" height=\"1197\" width=\"1800\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A SPAD XIII at the National Museum of the US Air Force in Dayton, Ohio.\n<p class=\"copyright\">US Air Force</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>World War I was the first combat experience for American pilots, who were then part of the Aeronautical Division of the US Signal Corps.</p><p>When the US entered the war in 1917, it was \"almost totally unprepared in aeronautical experience, equipment, and personnel,\" according to a post-war <a href=\"https://books.google.com/books/about/Unification_of_the_War_and_Navy_Departme.html?id=-DdqugEACAAJ\" target=\"_top\">report</a>.</p><p>With no experience or fighter aircraft of its own, the US had to purchase British- and French-made fighters. The most well-known was the <a href=\"https://airandspace.si.edu/collection-objects/spad-xiii-smith-iv/nasm_A19200001000\" target=\"_top\">SPAD XIII</a>.</p><p>The SPAD XIII was a French biplane armed with two Vickers machine guns that used <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/wwi-fighter-planes-fired-through-propeller-without-hitting-it-2019-5\" target=\"_top\">an interrupter gear to fire</a><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/wwi-fighter-planes-fired-through-propeller-without-hitting-it-2019-5\" target=\"_top\"> through the propeller</a><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/wwi-fighter-planes-fired-through-propeller-without-hitting-it-2019-5\" target=\"_top\">s</a>. It could carry four 25-pound bombs and had a top speed of about 135 mph.</p><p>With over 8,000 built, the SPAD XIII was one of the most-produced fighters of the war and was the US's primary fighter. The two most successful US aces of the war, Capt. Eddie Rickenbacker and 2nd Lt. Frank Luke, scored most of their kills with SPAD XIIIs.</p><h2>P-38 Lightning and P-51 Mustang</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fa991ccf7d1cb0019e3a975?format=jpeg\" alt=\"P-38 Lightning fighter plane WWII\" height=\"1048\" width=\"1398\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>An early model of the Lockheed P-38 Lightning over Los Angeles, November 20, 1940.\n<p class=\"copyright\">(AP Photo)</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>By the time of World War II, US pilots, then part of the US Army Air Corps, were much better prepared.</p><p>US manufacturers had developed dozens of fighter designs. One was the <a href=\"https://www.lockheedmartin.com/en-us/news/features/history/p-38.html\" target=\"_top\">P-38 Lightning</a>, which was introduced in 1941 and was one of the fastest in the world, with a top speed over 400 mph. It was also used extensively for reconnaissance and obtained 90% of the aerial film recorded over Europe.</p><p>A P-38 was the first US fighter flown by an American<!-- First US fighter flown by an American or first US-made fighter flown by anyone? --><!-- First US fighter flown by an American. We had sent some other planes to the British before. --> to shoot down a German aircraft, and its success over Europe earned it the nickname \"the fork-tailed devil\" among Germans, referring to its distinctive twin-tail design.</p><p>The P-38 truly distinguished itself in the Pacific, however, claiming more Japanese aircraft than any other fighter. The two best US aces of the war, Maj. Richard Bong and Maj. Thomas McGuire, scored all of their victories with P-38s in the Pacific.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5cf0167c11e205490863ce25?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Air Force P-51 Mustang Spangdahlem Germany\" height=\"848\" width=\"1400\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A P-51 Mustang at Spangdahlem Air Base in Germany, May 28, 2019.\n<p class=\"copyright\">US Air Force/Staff Sgt. Preston Cherry</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>But the <a href=\"https://www.boeing.com/history/products/p-51-mustang.page\" target=\"_top\">P-51 Mustang</a> is perhaps the best-known American fighter of World War II. Introduced in 1942, it carried six M2 Browning .50-caliber machine guns in its wings. Racks under the wings could carry 10 rockets or up to 1,000 pounds of bombs.</p><p>The Mustang could reach 425 mph and 40,000 feet, and was the US's primary fighter in Europe, though it also served as a fighter-bomber.</p><p>P-51s are <a href=\"https://www.af.mil/News/Photos/igphoto/2000593917/\" target=\"_top\">believed</a> to have shot down 4,950 enemy aircraft. They were so successful and so numerous (over 15,000 built) that British planes were able to resume daylight bombing raids on Germany in 1944 with P-51s escorting them the whole way.</p><p>A Senate committee called it \"the most aerodynamically perfect pursuit plane in existence,\" and Hermann Göring, who commanded Germany's air force, reportedly <a href=\"https://www.google.com/books/edition/Fighter_Aces/xDouDwAAQBAJ?hl=en&gbpv=0pv=0\" target=\"_top\">said</a> after the war that \"when I saw Mustangs over Berlin, I knew the jig was up.\"</p><p>The P-51 was the main US fighter until the F-86 Sabre arrived in 1949, but it continued to serve in the Korean War.</p><h2>F-86 Sabre</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/56619c3fc28144c1018b7606?format=jpeg\" alt=\"f 86 sabre korean war\" height=\"794\" width=\"1457\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A three-ship North American F-86F Sabre formation during the Korean War in 1953.\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/North_American_F-86_Sabre#/media/File:Col_Ben_O._Davis_leads_F-86_flight_%2851st_FIW,_Korea%29.jpg\" target=\"_blank\">USAF</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>The Sabre wasn't the Air Force's first jet fighter, but none of its predecessors could handle the Soviet-made MiG-15 when the Korean War started in 1950.</p><p>As a result, the Sabre was rushed to the front line. Armed with six .50-caliber machine guns and 16 rockets, the Sabre's top speed was 650 mph and its service ceiling<!-- Is service ceiling different from operational ceiling? --><!-- As far as I know the only official terms are service ceiling and absolute ceiling. I have seen operational ceiling being used as a substitute for service ceiling. I changed where I put operational just now to solve the confusion. Apologies.  --> was over 45,000 feet.</p><p>Its excellent maneuverability, combined with the fact that most US pilots were hardened World War II veterans, enabled the Sabre to wreak havoc on North Korean, Chinese, and Soviet pilots.</p><p>Sabres shot down hundreds of MiGs. One post-war <a href=\"https://www.defenseindustrydaily.com/files/2008_RAND_Pacific_View_Air_Combat_Briefing.pdf\" target=\"_top\">study</a> put the loss ratio at almost 2:1. All but one of the American aces of the Korean War flew F-86s.</p><h2>F-4 Phantom II</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/56ec259c91058425008b74ba?format=jpeg\" alt=\"F 4 phantom camo\" height=\"1611\" width=\"2496\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>F-4 Phantom II fighters in formation during a heritage flight demonstration.\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Category:Aircraft_camouflage#/media/File:1997_F-4_Heritage_Flight_over_Florida-edit_1.jpg\" target=\"_blank\">USAF - MSgt Michael Ammons</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>In 1960, the US Navy adopted a new jet, the <a href=\"https://www.boeing.com/history/products/f-4-phantom-ii.page\" target=\"_top\">F-4 Phantom II</a>. Unlike its predecessors, the Phantom was designed as a fighter-bomber, allowing the Navy to field one model for multiple missions.</p><p>The Air Force adopted the F-4C variant in 1963. It was a twin-seat fighter-bomber capable of carrying up to 15,983 pounds of ordnance. It usually carried eight air-to-air missiles and eight 750-pound bombs.</p><p>The Phantom II was equipped with afterburners that made its top speed 1,485 mph, though it usually cruised at 590 mph. Its service ceiling was 56,100 feet.</p><p>It was the Vietnam War's defining jet. Air Force F-4Cs, with their speed and advanced radar, shot down 78% of the MiGs downed by the Air Force during the war. Only 33 of the 445 Phantoms the Air Force lost during the war were downed in aerial combat.</p><h2>F-15 Eagle and F-16 Fighting Falcon</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5bf4448010114219d763d46d?format=jpeg\" alt=\"F-16 Falcons for close air support, F-15E Strike Eagles for bombing missions and F-15 Eagle Fighters for combat air patrol\" height=\"1231\" width=\"2000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>F-15 Eagles, F-15E Strike Eagles, and F-16 Falcons during the first Gulf War.\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"http://www.apimages.com/metadata/Index/AP-I-KWT-KUWAIT-F-16/168ea1e4a8e0da11af9f0014c2589dfb/1/0\" target=\"_blank\">AP</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>With the lessons of Vietnam, the Air Force was determined to keep the advantage in fighter technology. The future of aerial warfare required fast, cost-effective fighters that could dominate the skies while striking ground targets.</p><p>The result was the <a href=\"https://www.af.mil/About-Us/Fact-Sheets/Display/Article/104501/f-15-eagle/\" target=\"_top\">F-15 Eagle</a> and the <a href=\"https://www.af.mil/About-Us/Fact-Sheets/Display/Article/104505/f-16-fighting-falcon/\" target=\"_top\">F-16 Fighting Falcon</a>. The F-15 was adopted in 1976 and the F-16 in 1978.</p><p>The F-15 was originally designed to carry eight air-to-air missiles, but <a href=\"https://www.popularmechanics.com/military/aviation/a22355833/boeing-new-f-15x/\" target=\"_top\">later models</a> could carry up to two dozen. It also has a 20 mm rotary cannon, and some variants can carry 23,000 pounds of ordnance.</p><p>The F-16, designed as a lightweight fighter, has a 20 mm rotary cannon and can carry eight missiles and up to 8,000 pounds of bombs.</p><p>Both are capable of speeds over 1,500 mph and can fly as high as 65,000 feet.</p><p>The F-15 has one of the best <a href=\"https://warisboring.com/has-anyone-ever-shot-down-an-f-15-in-air-combat/\" target=\"_top\">reputations</a> among fighter jets. Boeing claims it has never been shot down by enemy aircraft, giving it a remarkable kill ratio of 104:0. (Israel's air force is mostly responsible for that tally.) The F-16 is also <a href=\"https://nationalinterest.org/blog/buzz/meet-f-16-fighting-falcon-old-fighter-jet-keeps-killing-73676\" target=\"_top\">highly regarded</a>.</p><p>Though they were designed and built in the Cold War, the F-15 and F-16 remain the backbone of the Air Force's fighter fleet.</p><h2>F-22 Raptor and F-35 Lightning II</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5ade14ae7708e907c63c58f7?format=jpeg\" alt=\"F-35 and F-22\" height=\"3280\" width=\"4928\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Two F-22s and two F-35s.\n<p class=\"copyright\">USAF</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>As the Cold War ended, a new type of fighter was being created with an emphasis on speed, maneuverability, and a new characteristic — stealth. They were built with new angled designs, radar-absorbent material, and new electronics that made it harder for radar to spot.</p><p>The first, the <a href=\"https://www.airforce-technology.com/projects/f22a-raptor/\" target=\"_top\">F-22 Raptor</a>, was adopted in 2005. Its internal weapons bays can hold up to eight air-to-air missiles or two 1,000-pound bombs. Four external hardpoints allow it to carry more missiles or more than 9,00<!-- 900 or 9,000? --><!-- 9,000 -->0 pounds of ordnance. It also has a 20 mm rotary cannon.</p><p>The second, the <a href=\"https://www.f35.com/about\" target=\"_top\">F-35 Lightning II</a>, was adopted in 2016. It carries a <a href=\"https://www.f35.com/about/carrytheload/weaponry\" target=\"_top\">similar </a><a href=\"https://www.f35.com/about/carrytheload/weaponry\" target=\"_top\">payload</a>.</p><p>Neither have faced enemy fighters head-to-head, but they have had <a href=\"https://nationalinterest.org/blog/reboot/unbeatable-f-35-keeps-winning-war-game-after-war-game-168452\" target=\"_top\">promising results</a> in numerous simulations. They've also bombed ISIS targets in Syria.</p><p>The US relies on F-22s and F-35s to check rivals around the world, and they've been deployed to important US bases in Japan, Korea, and the United Arab Emirates.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a href='https://www.businessinsider.com/the-fighter-planes-and-jets-the-us-military-has-used-2020-11'>Business
