59-767_740defb435ea442b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=1J0lA_2Msdk:TyQcnfEglCk:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn15@2020_4/2020/11/12/04-49-56-681_6811756df77cc36f.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/1J0lA_2Msdk":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx25/cdn44@2020_5/2020/11/12/04-49-56-024_ba17fcd2cfb3bcd8.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1605156579244},{"createdTime":"2020-11-12 But retailers like Walmart aren't waiting until then to start marking down products. Online and in stores, Walmart is one of the most popular retailers to shop during Black Friday. This year, you can once again expect great deals on all the products you need for gifting and personal use.</p><p>Today, Walmart's second round of deals go live. Below, you'll find answers to frequently asked questions, plus when you can start shopping.&#160;</p><bi-shortcode id=\"table-of-contents-sticky\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-type=\"h2\">Table of Contents: Masthead Sticky</bi-shortcode><h2>Best early Black Friday 2020 deals from Walmart</h2><h3>November 11 at 7 p.m. EST online and in-store on November 14</h3><div id=\"ProductCard_5f986f77851d5a0bdd44a3e9\" style=\"position:relative; display:block; width: 100%\"><iframe src=\"https://produktor.businessinsider.com/productCardService?id=5f986f77851d5a0bdd44a3e9&type=medium&live=true\" width=\"100%\" height=\"150%\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"\" style=\"position:absolute; top:0; left: 0\"></iframe></div><div id=\"ProductCard_5f987076acfefb65d04a5d0c\" style=\"position:relative; display:block; width: 100%\"><iframe src=\"https://produktor.businessinsider.com/productCardService?id=5f987076acfefb65d04a5d0c&type=medium&live=true\" width=\"100%\" height=\"150%\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"\" style=\"position:absolute; top:0; left: 0\"></iframe></div><div id=\"ProductCard_5dadabb2cc4a0a3f1175f5c3\" style=\"position:relative; display:block; width: 100%\"><iframe src=\"https://produktor.businessinsider.com/productCardService?id=5dadabb2cc4a0a3f1175f5c3&type=medium&live=true\" width=\"100%\" height=\"150%\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"\" style=\"position:absolute; top:0; left: 0\"></iframe></div><h2>When does Walmart's Black Friday sale start?&#160;</h2><p>Walmart, like many retailers, is trying something new for <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/black-friday-deals\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Black Friday 2020</a> and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/cyber-monday-deals\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Cyber Monday 2020</a>. Instead of a weekend of markdowns and deals, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/walmart-black-friday-stores-limited-capacity-3-day-event-2020-10\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Walmart will stagger its offers</a> and introduce new ones every week until Black Friday. Here's the schedule:</p><ul><li>November 11 at 7 p.m. EST online and in-store on November 14 at 5 a.m. local time. Discounts will primarily be for TVs, smartphones, and tablets.</li><li>November 25 at 7 p.m. EST online and in-store on Black Friday, November 27 at 5 a.m. local time. This is the official Black Friday date, so we expect to see discounts on most categories.</li></ul><p>These sales end the day they are released. So if you miss a deal online, you'll have another opportunity in-store after a couple of days.</p><h2>How do we select the best Black Friday deals at Walmart?</h2><ul><li>We only choose products that meet our high standard of coverage, from brands we've tested and trust.</li><li>We compare the prices against other retailers like Amazon, Target, and Best Buy and only include the deals that are the same or better (not including promotional discounts that come from using certain credit cards).</li><li>We research price history thoroughly, to ensure that every deal we list is actually worth your time.</li></ul><h2>Can you shop at Walmart in person this year?</h2><p>Yes, but don't expect the mad rush during Black Friday like in years past. This year, Walmart will also limit store capacity to just 20% during its Black Friday sales. Plus, there will be safety precautions, including masks for staff and shoppers, plus carts will be sanitized.&#160;</p><p>Since Walmart scheduled each set of discounts online a few days in advance, shoppers should consider heading in-store only when they miss a deal.&#160;&#160;</p><h2>Does Walmart have curbside pickup?</h2><p>Every year around the holiday season, shipping delays and lost packages present a big headache for many consumers. To help alleviate that stress, Walmart offers contact-free curbside pickup for online orders. Going this route can save shoppers from any shipping-related headaches, so you'll have your orders on hand much sooner than if shipped.</p><h2>What early Black Friday deals should you buy at Walmart?</h2><p>Historically, Walmart's Black Friday markdowns are on par with those offered by Best Buy, Target, and Amazon — and this year is no different. Outside of a few select doorbusters, we expect each retailer to <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/stores-that-price-match\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">price-match their competitor's prices</a> during Black Friday.&#160; Shoppers can expect big savings on several TVs, streaming media players, kitchen appliances, and more.&#160;</p><p>With their staggered release, shoppers should shop for the deals offered during the aforementioned dates. Every deal that's been announced is either live right now and listed above or expired.</p><h3>&#160;</h3><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a 2020 00:07:00 Bufete)","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://i.insider.com/5fa472851df1d500182192aa?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx14/cdn32@2020_1/2020/11/12/04-50-02-731_3d527fde13daa26f.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn11@2020_1/2020/11/12/04-50-05-069_cc3ef43fc8ff5801.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=u8zOzF6v33E:2qsohErh8uc:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn67@2020_4/2020/11/12/04-49-57-162_d1f8d887b12df346.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=u8zOzF6v33E:2qsohErh8uc:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn75@2020_6/2020/11/12/04-49-53-763_47249ad1c74c4bff.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn48@2020_5/2020/11/12/04-49-59-767_740defb435ea442b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=u8zOzF6v33E:2qsohErh8uc:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn44@2020_6/2020/11/12/04-50-07-899_7ca1ecdaa5df4273.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/u8zOzF6v33E":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx3/cdn88@2020_3/2020/11/12/04-49-54-617_31b0cf7b91b6fb12.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1605156579252},{"createdTime":"2020-11-12 brightness","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-turn-on-flashlight-on-iphone","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac535a7f8f4200182a65f2?format=jpeg\" alt=\"kids playing with toys using phone flashlight telling stories\" height=\"1249\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>It&#39;s easy to turn on your iPhone&#39;s flashlight with a few taps or a voice command.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Annie Otzen/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>You can quickly turn on the flashlight on your iPhone by using Siri or the Control Center.</li>\n<li>The flashlight on your iPhone comes from the camera flash mechanism on the back of your device, next to the camera lens.&#160;</li>\n<li>You can also adjust the brightness of your iPhone flashlight in the Control Center.</li>\n<li><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tech-reference\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"summary_bullets\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"0\">Visit Business Insider's Tech Reference library for more stories</a>.</strong></li>\n</ul><p>In case you didn't know, the LED camera flash on your <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/category/iphone\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">iPhone</a> (as well as on your <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/category/ipad-pro\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">iPad Pro</a> and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/category/ipod-touch\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">iPod Touch</a>) doubles as a flashlight, a convenient feature that you can use while walking your dog at night, looking for small objects that have fallen underneath your bed, and more.&#160;</p><p>Here's how it's done.</p><h2><strong>How to turn your iPhone flashlight on or off using Siri</strong></h2><p><strong>1.</strong> To turn on your flashlight, say, \"Hey Siri, turn on my flashlight,\" or a similar phrase.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac4fbdb09abb0018626150?format=jpeg\" alt=\"IMG_5646.PNG\" height=\"2208\" width=\"1242\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Say &#34;Hey Siri, turn flashlight on.&#34;\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abigail Abesamis Demarest/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>2.</strong> To turn off your flashlight, say, \"Hey Siri, turn off my flashlight,\" or a similar phrase.</p><p><strong>3.</strong> If you have the \"Listen for 'Hey Siri'\" feature disabled, press and hold the power button for iPhones with Face ID or press and hold the home button before speaking these commands.</p><h2><strong>How to turn your iPhone flashlight on or off using the Control Center</strong></h2><p><strong>1.</strong> For iPhones with Face ID, swipe down from the upper right corner of the screen to open the Control Center. For iPhones without Face ID, swipe up from the bottom of the screen to open the Control Center.</p><p><strong>2.</strong> Tap the flashlight icon to turn on the flashlight. Tap the flashlight icon again to turn off the flashlight.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac506d7f8f4200182a65db?format=jpeg\" alt=\"flashlight1\" height=\"1504\" width=\"1216\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Tap the flashlight icon to turn it on and off.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abigail Abesamis Demarest/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>3.</strong> You can also turn on the flashlight from the Lock screen. For iPhones with Face ID, press and hold the flashlight icon in the bottom left corner. For iPhones without Face ID, swipe up from the bottom of the screen to open the Control Center.</p><h2><strong>How to change the brightness of an iPhone flashlight</strong></h2><p><strong>1.</strong> For iPhones with Face ID, swipe down from the upper right corner of the screen to open the Control Center. For iPhones without Face ID, swipe up from the bottom of the screen to open the Control Center.</p><p><strong>2.</strong> Press and hold the flashlight icon.</p><p><strong>3.</strong> Tap or slide your finger along the vertical bar to turn the brightness up and down.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac50f9b09abb0018626159?format=jpeg\" alt=\"IMG_5643.PNG\" height=\"2208\" width=\"1242\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Swipe your finger up or down to adjust the flashlight&#39;s brightness.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abigail Abesamis Demarest/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><div id=\"ProductCard_5d8e19fb2e22af18f40d281d\" style=\"position:relative; display:block; width: 100%\"><iframe href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B074VJYRZN/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=biip_110920_samsonite-centric-luggage-review-20&camp=1789&creative=9325&linkCode=as2&creativeASIN=B074VJYRZN&linkId=558821a6f4a565292cc9261570a9a02cf4a565292cc9261570a9a02c\" src=\"https://produktor.businessinsider.com/productCardService?id=5f734e77d67e123b3026cc8e&type=small&live=true\" width=\"100%\" height=\"150%\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"\" style=\"position:absolute; top:0; left: 0\"></iframe></div><bi-shortcode id=\"table-of-contents-sticky\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-type=\"h2\">Table of Contents: Masthead Sticky</bi-shortcode><p>A solid and reliable carry-on is an essential piece of luggage for any traveler. Key factors that make a carry-on suitcase standout are size, weight, durability, and how easy it is to pack. As a travel editor, I've tested numerous carry-ons over the years, including for our guide to the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-carry-on-bag\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">best carry-on suitcases</a>.&#160;</p><p>The <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B074VJYRZN/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=biip_110920_samsonite-centric-luggage-review-20&camp=1789&creative=9325&linkCode=as2&creativeASIN=B074VJYRZN&linkId=558821a6f4a565292cc9261570a9a02cf4a565292cc9261570a9a02c\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Samsonite Centric 20\" Hardside Expandable Luggage with Spinner Wheels</a> beat out the competition and is my top overall pick as the best hard-side carry-on bag you can buy. I've used this suitcase on trips ranging from lengthy international vacations to quick weekend getaways and found that it excels when it comes to function, durability, and ease of use. Plus, it comes in at an excellent price point for the quality. After several years of use, this suitcase continues to impress me.</p><h2>Design and specs</h2><p>The most important factor when it comes to a carry-on is that it fits in an airplane's overhead bin. After all, if you get to your seat and discover that your bag won't fit, the whole point of packing a carry-on has been defeated.&#160;</p><p>While this bag is specifically noted as being 20 inches in height, it's important to understand that measurement actually refers to interior packable space. The overall height of the exterior of the bag actually comes in at 22 inches, including the wheels, when I measured it. Luckily, this is still well within the FAA sizing regulations and, in my experience, this bag easily fits on nearly all international and domestic flights, with the exception of tiny jumper planes.&#160;</p><p>The hard-side suitcase is made out of high-quality polycarbonate. The twill texture is scratch- and scuff-resistant with a slightly shiny finish. This bag weighs 7.5 pounds, which is pretty average in terms of carry-ons and it's easy enough to lift into overhead bins. Standout details also include rubberized grip under the top and side handles for extra comfort when lifting the bag, smooth silver zippers that are easy to grip and pull, and a TSA-approved lock.</p><p>The four multi-directional wheels are also excellent. They are quiet and the suitcase rolls in front of you, beside you, or behind you on almost any surface easily. However, they are not as functional on thick carpet as some of the best wheels I've tested on other bags. That said, I haven't come across too many instances during my travels when I actually needed to pull the bag on thick carpet, so that has not been a significant issue.&#160;&#160;</p><p><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B074VJYRZN/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=biip_110920_samsonite-centric-luggage-review-20&camp=1789&creative=9325&linkCode=as2&creativeASIN=B074VJYRZN&linkId=558821a6f4a565292cc9261570a9a02cf4a565292cc9261570a9a02c\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">The Samsonite Centric Hardside</a> carry-on is available in three colors: black, orange, and teal.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac4f207f8f4200182a65d0?format=jpeg\" alt=\"samsonite centric hardside luggage review zipper\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Hannah Freedman/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><h2>What it's like to use</h2><p>I've been using the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B074VJYRZN/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=biip_110920_samsonite-centric-luggage-review-20&camp=1789&creative=9325&linkCode=as2&creativeASIN=B074VJYRZN&linkId=558821a6f4a565292cc9261570a9a02cf4a565292cc9261570a9a02c\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Samsonite Centric Hardside Carry-On</a> for several years, and its best quality is how well it has held up over that time. While there are a few scuff marks visible if you really get up close to inspect the bag, they are minimal. There are no serious scratches or dents to speak of and from afar, the bag still looks practically new.</p><p>As previously mentioned, the wheels are a breeze on most surfaces and make the suitcase very easy to roll on and off the plane and through crowded airports. The adjustable handle is a good height, but it does wobble a decent amount and could be sturdier.&#160;</p><p>While 20 inches of interior space may not sound like a lot, I've been able to easily pack a week's worth of clothes in this carry-on for longer trips. The interiors don't offer any fancy perks, but the mesh zipper pocket and strong buckles are sufficient for securing clothes, shoes, and packing cubes in place. The handle poles do take up some space on one side of the bag, which can make laying clothes totally flat a challenge. However, if you pack smartly you can build yourself a base with smaller items and lay additional clothes flat on top of that.&#160;&#160;I like to pack shoes and items that need extra securing on the side with the mesh zipper, and bulkier items like sweaters on the opposite side so I can pull the buckles tight to help compress them.</p><p>This suitcase also has the option to expand by unzipping extra zippers on the outside. While I don't recommend using the expandable option if you know you'll be on smaller planes, I do like the versatility it allows. I've used the expandable option on longer international and cross-country flights when I know the overhead bins will easily accommodate the bag even at a slightly larger width. It is also a nice feature for travelers like me who tend to always pick up a souvenir or two and need extra room for them on the trip home.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac4f3f7f8f4200182a65d3?format=jpeg\" alt=\"samsonite centric hardside luggage review interior\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Hannah Freedman/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><h2>What makes the Samsonite Centric Hardside carry-on stand out</h2><p>The value of this bag is what really sets it apart. The materials are of good quality and highly durable and will last for years. While many high-end suitcases easily come in closer to $300 or more, this suitcase starts around $150 and frequently can be found on sale for under $100, making it an excellent value.</p><p>While this suitcase doesn't come with many bells and whistles, it has everything you need for a good, sturdy carry-on and comes in at the right price.</p><h2>The cons</h2><p>The biggest downside of the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B074VJYRZN/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=biip_110920_samsonite-centric-luggage-review-20&camp=1789&creative=9325&linkCode=as2&creativeASIN=B074VJYRZN&linkId=558821a6f4a565292cc9261570a9a02cf4a565292cc9261570a9a02c\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Samsonite Centric</a> is the adjustable handle. While it's held up fine over the past few years, it is very wobbly and much less sturdy when compared to the handles of other high-end suitcases.</p><p>This carry-on is also a pretty standard weight at 7.5 pounds. While it hasn't been an issue for me, if you have trouble lifting carry-ons or tend to overpack and worry about every last ounce for the weigh-in required on some flights, you may be better suited to a lightweight carry-on option.&#160;</p><p>This suitcase is also fairly bare-bones and doesn't come with any extras like a USB port or extra interior organizers.&#160;</p><h2>The bottom line</h2><p>There are seemingly endless options when it comes to carry-on suitcases, and undoubtedly there are other hard-side options on the market worth considering, including the <a href=\"https://go.skimresources.com?id=35871X943606&xs=1&url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bloomingdales.com%2Fshop%2Fproduct%2Frimowa-essential-lite-cabin-small%3FID%3D3141780D3141780\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Rimowa Essential Lite</a> ($490), the <a href=\"https://www.gopjn.com/t/TUJGRkpGSUJGSEhLR01CRkpKS0ZJ?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.awaytravel.com%2Fsuitcases%2Fcarry-on%2Fcoast\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Away Carry-On </a>($225), and the <a href=\"https://www.tumi.com/p/international-carry-on-0287660NVY/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Tumi International Carry-On</a> ($750). However, as you'll notice, nearly all of those will cost you significantly more. If you're looking for a suitcase that will last a lifetime or that comes with lots of extras, these suitcases might better suit your needs.&#160;</p><p>But for a quality bag that is durable and will last you several years without breaking the bank, the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B074VJYRZN/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=biip_110920_samsonite-centric-luggage-review-20&camp=1789&creative=9325&linkCode=as2&creativeASIN=B074VJYRZN&linkId=558821a6f4a565292cc9261570a9a02cf4a565292cc9261570a9a02c\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Samsonite Centric 20\" Hardside Expandable Luggage with Spinner Wheels</a> is tough to beat. This suitcase has all the qualities you need in a solid carry-on, including plenty of packing space, a durable and scratch-resistant shell, excellent multi-directional wheels, an expansion option, and the right dimensions to fit in almost any overhead bin.&#160;</p><p><strong>Pros:</strong> Excellent price for the quality, durable, scratch-resistant, wheels easily, expandable</p><p><strong>Cons:</strong> Handle wiggles a decent amount when fully extended, slightly heavier than other options available&#160;</p><div id=\"ProductCard_5f734e77d67e123b3026cc8e\" +0000","feedId":22,"bgimg":"https://i.insider.com/5f7c96d9282c500018c78dc8?format=jpeg","linkMd5":"e28ae45e0975c22142778ad4d68e9539","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn10@2020_1/2020/11/12/04-49-49-621_c047dc1df349eceb.webp","destWidth":1667,"destHeight":1250,"sourceBytes":181084,"destBytes":181084,"author":"hfreedman@businessinsider.com (Hannah Freedman)","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://i.insider.com/5f7c96d9282c500018c78dc8?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn10@2020_1/2020/11/12/04-49-49-621_c047dc1df349eceb.webp","https://i.insider.com/5fac4f207f8f4200182a65d0?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn84@2020_2/2020/11/12/04-49-56-664_bcf714f1894fea7f.webp","https://i.insider.com/5fac4f3f7f8f4200182a65d3?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn96@2020_1/2020/11/12/04-49-55-597_ca1dbdf24531fa7d.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn11@2020_1/2020/11/12/04-50-05-069_cc3ef43fc8ff5801.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=63FhnXOb5Do:2Mz8t-cLqcc:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx3/cdn24@2020_3/2020/11/12/04-50-07-710_9fad09a84ab8d936.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=63FhnXOb5Do:2Mz8t-cLqcc:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn40@2020_6/2020/11/12/04-50-04-968_bd1498664dbf785d.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn48@2020_5/2020/11/12/04-49-59-767_740defb435ea442b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=63FhnXOb5Do:2Mz8t-cLqcc:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn59@2020_4/2020/11/12/04-50-04-388_3c1cd1d5ece45daa.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/63FhnXOb5Do":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx25/cdn36@2020_3/2020/11/12/04-50-05-306_c0a2a683a0fbd67a.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1605156579253},{"createdTime":"2020-11-12 12:49:39","updatedTime":"2020-11-12 12:49:39","title":"In the Trump campaign's latest election lawsuit, Republican poll watchers complain they couldn't stand within 6 feet of poll workers because of coronavirus guidelines","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/trump-michigan-election-lawsuit-poll-watchers-social-distancing-complaints-2020-11","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac584e98669500182b57fe?format=jpeg\" alt=\"donald trump hands\" height=\"1907\" width=\"2542\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>President Donald Trump.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Alex Wong/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>The Trump campaign announced a new 342-page lawsuit on Tuesday night challenging the election process in Michigan.</li>\n<li>The lawsuit doesn't make a single specific claim of voter fraud or electoral fraud but says the state's votes shouldn't be certified anyway.</li>\n<li>Much of the lawsuit is composed of affidavits from GOP election observers. More than a dozen of them complained they were told to stay more than 6 feet away from ballot counters because of the coronavirus pandemic.</li>\n<li>Justin Levitt, an elections expert, told Insider it wouldn't make sense to invalidate the election results based on the arguments in the lawsuit: \"It would be like demanding that because I was impeded from checking to see whether a car were parked over the metered time, we should blow up the car,\" he said.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>The Trump campaign announced <a href=\"https://beta.documentcloud.org/documents/20404059-trump-campaign-election-lawsuit-michigan-federal\">a new lawsuit Tuesday night</a>, alleging widespread problems with the electoral process in Michigan, a state President Donald Trump lost to President-elect Joe Biden by more than 145,000 votes.</p><p>The lawsuit, which has not yet been filed, says the campaign's election observers were forced to stay more than 6 feet away from election workers in Wayne County — a social-distancing measure put in place because of the coronavirus pandemic that's <a href=\"https://coronavirus.jhu.edu/us-map\">killed more than 238,000 people in the US</a>.</p><p>But the lawsuit alleges the distancing also meant \"Republican challengers were not allowed to meaningfully observe the ballot counting process.\" The lawsuit claims that, compounded with other irregularities with the ballot-counting process, means Wayne County didn't properly follow Michigan's election laws.</p><p>Trump's campaign is asking a federal court to stop Wayne County — where Trump is behind by more than 323,000 votes, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/2020-election-results\">according to Decision Desk HQ data published by Insider</a>, and which includes the city of Detroit — from certifying a swath of its votes until those irregularities are fixed and a number of the ballots are counted again.</p><p>The Trump campaign does not challenge the validity of Wayne County's votes or allege a single case of voter fraud or electoral fraud.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5faa71961df1d50018219c6d?format=jpeg\" alt=\"poll workers detroit\" height=\"1333\" width=\"1778\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Poll workers in Detroit on November 3.\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://www.gettyimages.com/detail/news-photo/poll-worker-prepares-to-start-counting-ballots-during-the-news-photo/1229468285?adppopup=true\" target=\"_blank\">Salwan Georges/The Washington Post via Getty Images</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>A victory in this lawsuit is unlikely to substantially change the state's vote count and risk Biden's electoral victory in Michigan, Justin Levitt, a professor at Loyola Law School, told Insider.</p><p style=\"font-weight: 400;\">\"You can't throw out an election because you just guess that there might have been wrongdoing maybe, particularly when there's no other reason to suspect any misconduct,\" Levitt said. \"I don't believe Michigan law requires the election officials be supervised every step of the way by observers. Even if it did, that still wouldn't be cause to overturn the actual votes cast.\"</p><p style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Even if Biden were to somehow lose Michigan's 16 electoral votes, his <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/2020-election-results\">projected victories in other states</a> would still grant him enough electoral votes for the presidency.</p><p><a href=\"https://beta.documentcloud.org/documents/20404059-trump-campaign-election-lawsuit-michigan-federal\">The 342-page complaint</a> includes dozens of affidavits from election workers working with the Trump campaign and Republican Party. Of those people who signed affidavits, 14 complained about the 6-foot rule, saying it was too far for them to properly observe ballot processing.</p><p>\"On numerous occasions I was told by poll workers that I needed to stay six feet from them. When I asked if I could come closer because I could not see the screen to verify whether the voter and ballot numbers matched I was told I could not,\" says a typical passage from one affidavit by a woman who identified herself as a Republican Party poll challenger.</p><p>Levitt, a former Justice Department official who oversaw voting-rights cases, told Insider that the complaints about access didn't necessarily have merit, since the election has safeguards beyond just partisan observers.</p><p>\"It's up to elections officials in the first instance to test the validity of the ballots, and there are lots of safeguards beyond third-party observers to make sure election officials do their job,\" he told Insider. \"It does not follow that every procedural glitch means that you invalidate the election or toss out legitimate ballots.\"</p><h2>Other people who signed affidavits didn't mention problems with standing 6 feet away</h2><p>Three other people who signed affidavits for the lawsuit — Jeffrey Moss, Erik Duus, and Jeremy McCall — said they were asked to stand 6 feet away from election workers, but they did not say the distance prevented them from properly observing anything and suggested they were able to view irregularities from a distance.</p><p>Another person, Randall S. Champagne, said staying 6 feet away made it difficult for him to observe but that he saw irregularities anyway and wasn't close enough to formally challenge them.</p><p>Marc Russell, another poll challenger, signed an affidavit saying he was told to stand 6 feet away from people but that the workers counting ballots were not. He didn't say what problem he had with standing 6 feet apart from others.</p><div class=\"insider-raw-embed\"><iframe\n  src=\"https://embed.documentcloud.org/documents/20404059-trump-campaign-election-lawsuit-michigan-federal/?embed=1&title=1le=1\"\n  title=\"Trump Campaign election lawsuit Michigan federal (Hosted by DocumentCloud)\"\n  width=\"700\"\n  height=\"905\"\n  style=\"border: 1px solid #aaa;\"\n  sandbox=\"allow-scripts allow-same-origin allow-popups allow-forms\"\n></iframe></div><p>Angela Marie Eilf testified in her affidavit that she was told she'd have to keep 6 feet of distance from others and properly wear a mask. She said she was \"immediately concerned by these instructions\" but did not say why. Her affidavit didn't list any problems with the ballot-counting process.</p><p>One person, Mindi Tietz, alleged she was told she needed to stand 20 feet away from the people counting ballots.</p><p>Some of the people who signed affidavits for the lawsuit also made baseless speculations about irregularities, Reuters' Brad Heath said.</p><blockquote class=\"twitter-tweet blockquote\" data-lang=\"en\" data-cards=\"\" data-conversation=\"none\">&#8212;Brad Heath  (@bradheath) <a href=\"https://twitter.com/mims/statuses/1326396394891079681?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw\">November src=\"//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"></script><p>Levitt told Insider that many of the claims represented in the lawsuit went beyond what partisan election observers are supposed to do.</p><p>\"Just because the observers decide that's their job doesn't mean it's so, any more than I can decide it's my job to go out and issue parking tickets if I think I see a car parked over the metered time,\" he said.</p><p>He said it wouldn't make any sense to invalidate any ballots based on the allegations in the lawsuit.</p><p>\"Continuing my extended analogy, it would be like demanding that because I was impeded from checking to see whether a car were parked over the metered time, we should blow up the car (without any actual evidence that the car was in fact illegally parked),\" he said.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fa307cf69331a0011bc752c?format=jpeg\" alt=\"trump michigan lawsuit\" height=\"1666\" width=\"2222\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Police and election officials as Detroit election workers count absentee ballots for the 2020 election.\n<p class=\"copyright\">JEFF KOWALSKY/AFP via Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>The Michigan secretary of state's office, which oversees the election process in the state, didn't immediately respond to Insider's request for comment on Wednesday.</p><p>It's not clear why the lawsuit hasn't appeared in PACER, the database of federal court records, nearly a day after the Trump campaign announced it. The campaign didn't immediately respond to a request for comment.</p><p>The new federal lawsuit recycles several claims from a failed suit the campaign filed in a Michigan state court earlier in November. In that lawsuit, the campaign also alleged that the lack of access for some election observers violated the law. <a href=\"https://beta.documentcloud.org/documents/20404391-opinion-and-order-in-state-michigan-trump-election-case\">Judge Cynthia Stephens threw the case out</a>, saying the allegations were too vague and that the ballot-counting process was over by that time anyway.</p><p>The new lawsuit is <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trump-campaign-lawsuits-election-results-2020-11\">one of many</a>&#160;Trump is bringing across the country to challenge the election results. In Pennsylvania, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trump-campaign-lawsuit-pennsylvania-votes-biden-enough-win-2020-11\">he filed a federal lawsuit</a> challenging the state's entire Electoral College count on similar grounds. And in the Supreme Court, he seeks to join a lawsuit that would disqualify the roughly 10,000 Pennsylvania ballots that were mailed in by Election Day but arrived at ballot-processing centers afterward.</p><p>In <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trump-campaign-lawsuits-election-results-2020-11\">another earlier lawsuit</a> in Pennsylvania, the Trump campaign sued over distancing measures for its election observers.</p><p>It won the lawsuit, successfully obtaining permission for the observers to stand no less than 6 feet away from poll workers.</p><p><strong>Read more:</strong></p><p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trump-campaign-lawsuit-pennsylvania-votes-biden-enough-win-2020-11\" data-read-more-link=\"\" data-e2e-name=\"read-more-link\">Even if Trump wins his Pennsylvania ballot 'fraud' lawsuit, he'd invalidate only 14,000 votes — not nearly enough to stop a Biden presidency</a></p><p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trump-pennsylvania-election-lawsuit-allege-voter-fraud-2-counties-2020-11\" data-read-more-link=\"\" data-e2e-name=\"read-more-link\">Trump's big new election lawsuit alleges voter fraud potentially happened in 2 Pennsylvania counties. Both overwhelmingly voted for him.</a></p><p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trump-campaign-lawsuits-election-results-2020-11\">Here are the legal challenges Trump's campaign and Republicans have filed to contest the 2020 election results</a></p><p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/late-mail-ballots-supreme-court-case-wont-help-trump-2020-11\">Ballots arriving late in the mail 12:49:39","updatedTime":"2020-11-12 12:49:39","title":"How to delete a Craigslist post you've listed in 5 simple steps","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-delete-a-craigslist-post","description":"<figure> \n <img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fa9bb2c1df1d50018219b87?format=jpeg\" alt=\"shop owner woman selling online holding tablet\" height=\"1249\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\"> \n  <figcaption>\n   If you've created a Craigslist post, you can delete it at any time. \n   <p class=\"copyright\">Cavan Images/Getty Images</p> \n  </figcaption> </img>\n</figure>\n<ul class=\"summary-list\"> \n <li>You can easily delete a Craigslist post by accessing the email you used to make the listing.</li> \n <li>You can delete a post for any reason, including if you've sold an item or changed your mind about getting rid of it.</li> \n <li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tech-reference\"><strong>Visit Business Insider's Tech Reference library for more stories</strong></a><strong>.</strong></li> \n</ul>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/category/craigslist\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Craigslist</a> is an old-school site, with a simplified look and minimal features. Anyone with an email can list an apartment, job opportunity, or item for sale.&nbsp;</p>\n<p>Once your post has served its purpose, you'll want to delete it so people know your item or opportunity is no longer available. You'll just need to go to the original email you received when you first created your post.</p>\n<h2><strong>How to delete a Craigslist post</strong></h2>\n<p>Once you've created an ad, you'll be able to delete it at any time for any reason. After your ad goes live, Craigslist will send an automated email that includes the post's numerical ID and the title of your ad in the subject line. Here you'll find a link to your ad as well as a link to edit or delete your post.</p>\n<p><strong>1.</strong> Open your email inbox.</p>\n<p><strong>2.</strong> Search for the automated email from Craigslist. It should have come from <a href=\"mailto:robot@craiglist.org\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">robot@craigslist.org</a>.</p>\n<p><strong>3.</strong> Scroll to \"To edit or delete your ad, please visit the following URL, \" and click the link.</p>\n<figure> \n <img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fa9b687f7d1cb0019e3aa8e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How_to_delete_a_Craigslist_post_2\" height=\"1429\" width=\"2486\" charset=\"\"> \n  <figcaption>\n   In the email you received from Craigslist when you first created your post, click the link to edit or delete it. \n   <p class=\"copyright\">Vivian McCall/Business Insider</p> \n  </figcaption> </img>\n</figure>\n<p><strong>4.</strong> Enter the email and password you used to create the listing.</p>\n<p><strong>5.</strong> Click \"Delete this posting.\"</p>\n<figure> \n <img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fa9b7721df1d50018219b6b?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How_to_delete_a_Craigslist_post_3\" height=\"1423\" width=\"2542\" charset=\"\"> \n  <figcaption>\n   Click on \"Delete this Posting\" at the top of the screen. \n   <p class=\"copyright\">Vivian McCall/Business Insider</p> \n  </figcaption> </img>\n</figure>\n<p>If you've changed your mind, you can \"undelete\" the post by following the same link as above.</p>\n<figure> \n <img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fa9b8151df1d50018219b6f?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How_to_delete_a_Craigslist_post_4\" height=\"1416\" width=\"2503\" charset=\"\"> \n  <figcaption>\n   Click \"Undelete this Posting\" if you want to repost it. \n   <p class=\"copyright\">Vivian McCall/Business Insider</p> \n  </figcaption> </img>\n</figure>\n<h2><strong>Related coverage from&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tech-reference\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" It costs $69.99 and is sent as an email subscription card to your recipient on a date of your choosing. Learn more about the gift subscription below.&#160;</p><p><em>Updated on 11/11/2020 by Steven Cohen: Added details about the new Disney Plus GroupWatch feature, along with links to related articles and gift guides.</em></p><h2>Here's how to gift a Disney Plus annual subscription:</h2><ol><li><a href=\"https://disneyplus.bn5x.net/c/196318/734688/9358\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\">Visit this page to purchase the gift</a>.&#160;</li><li>You'll enter your information, your recipient's name and email, and what date you'd like the email to be delivered.&#160;</li><li>The $69.99 fee will be charged to your account as soon as you make the purchase.&#160;</li><li>Your recipient will visit DisneyPlus.com/redeememail, select the offer, and manually enter the code printed on the email.&#160;</li><li>Once redeemed, the recipient will be credited a one year subscription to Disney Plus.&#160;</li><li>If the recipient doesn't see the gift confirmation email in their inbox on the selected delivery date, Disney recommends that they check their spam folder. If the email still can't be located, you can contact Disney Plus customer service to have the code resent.</li></ol><h2>Restrictions of the Disney Plus gift subscription:</h2><ol><li>The gift subscription can only be redeemed by new Disney Plus subscribers.&#160;</li><li>The redemption code is one-time use only and non-transferable.&#160;</li></ol><h2>Once they've activated the subscription, your recipient will get:</h2><ul><li>Unlimited, ad-free access to thousands of movies and series from Disney, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/pixar-movies-on-disney-plus\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Pixar</a>, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/marvel-disney-plus\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Marvel</a>, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/star-wars-disney-plus\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Star Wars</a>, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/national-geographic-disney-plus\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">National Geographic</a>, and 20th Century Fox. This includes <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/new-movies-disney-plus\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\">original programming</a> exclusive to the Disney Plus platform, like the popular \"Star Wars\" show \"<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-watch-the-mandalorian\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">The Mandalorian</a>.\"&#160;</li><li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/disney-plus-app\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Unlimited downloads</a> they can watch anywhere, anytime.</li><li>The ability to stream on up to four devices simultaneously and add up to seven profiles.</li><li>A <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/disney-plus-groupwatch\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">GroupWatch</a> feature that allows them to sync and watch streams with friends and family virtually.</li></ul><h2>Can Disney Plus gift subscriptions be used for the bundle with ESPN+ and Hulu?</h2><p><a href=\"https://disneyplus.bn5x.net/c/196318/734688/9358\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Disney Plus gift vouchers</a>&#160;are only available for an annual subscription to Disney Plus, but recipients can still upgrade to the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/disney-plus-bundle\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">streaming bundle with Hulu and ESPN+</a> for a discounted price. Here's how to upgrade and save:</p><ol><li>Redeem your Disney Plus gift subscription voucher and create a Disney Plus account.</li><li>Visit the <a href=\"https://www.disneyplus.com/account/subscription\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Disney Plus Billing Details page</a> and choose the option to switch to the Disney bundle.</li><li>You will now be upgraded to the $12.99 per month bundle plan with Disney Plus, Hulu, and ESPN+.</li><li>A $5.83 monthly credit (the value of your gift subscription) will then be applied to the monthly bill for your bundle.</li><li>This will bring the bundle price down to $7.16 per month for the duration of you gift subscription period.</li></ol><div id=\"ProductCard_5df148b4fd9db276182c0665\" 12:49:39","updatedTime":"2020-11-12 12:49:39","title":"'Trump's not that person': Marine veteran and Gold Star widow says a president should understand what it means to serve and sacrifice","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/marine-vet-and-gold-star-widow-presidents-should-understand-service-2020-11","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac6e6098669500182b588e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Soldiers from the 3rd Infantry Regiment, also called the &#34;Old Guard,&#34; place US flags in front of every grave site in Arlington National Cemetery.\" height=\"287\" width=\"575\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Soldiers from the 3rd Infantry Regiment, also called the &#34;Old Guard,&#34; place US flags in front of every grave site in Arlington National Cemetery.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Chip Somodevilla/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Marine veteran and Gold Star widow Kait Wyatt, whose husband Derek was killed in combat, told Insider Wednesday that it is important that the commander-in-chief of the armed forces understand military service and sacrifice.</li>\n<li>She said that veterans \"put their lives on the line and soak up the negativity that is in our world so that they can shield the people who need it the most.\"</li>\n<li>Wyatt said that President Donald Trump has not demonstrated an understanding of that service while President-elect Joe Biden, a Blue Star family member, likely has a better grasp of what that means.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>A Marine Corps veteran and Gold Star widow stressed to Insider the importance of having a commander-in-chief that understands military service and sacrifice in an interview Wednesday.</p><p>Kait Wyatt and her husband Derek were in the Marines together, and during their service, Derek made the ultimate sacrifice. He was killed in combat in Afghanistan in 2010.</p><p>\"It has been 10 years, and we miss him every day,\" Wyatt said, \"I don't think that'll ever change.\"</p><p>Reflecting on Veteran's Day, Wyatt told Insider that it is \"not only honoring the sacrifice of the veteran but also bringing light to the struggle that it is to be in the military.\"</p><p>She characterized veterans, as well as people like first responders, as those that \"put their lives on the line and soak up the negativity that is in our world so that they can shield the people who need it the most.\" Wyatt argued that a president should have some understanding of what that service and sacrifice means.</p><p>\"Donald Trump's not that person,\" she said, adding that on the far end of the sliding scale of selfishness, \"there's Donald Trump, where the only thing that matters is Donald Trump.\"</p><p>During his presidency, Trump, who has suggested he would have made a good general but does not actually have military experience, has made a number of disparaging remarks about veterans and military families, such as late Arizona Sen. John McCain or Gold Star father Khizr Khan, among others.</p><p>There are also reports that Trump called troops killed in combat \"losers\" and \"suckers,\" as well as reports that he questioned a fallen Marine's service, telling the father at his son's grave in Arlington: \"I don't get it.\"</p><p>In an interview with CNN in September, Wyatt <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/gold-star-widow-blasts-trump-over-photo-at-arlington-cemetery-2020-9\">expressed anger and frustration after seeing a photo of Trump standing at her husband's grave at Arlington</a>. \"You can't stand on the graves of better men who fought and died for this country while you rip apart that country with your incompetence and unqualified presence within a position of leadership,\" she told CNN.</p><p>Trump visited Arlington National Cemetery again Wednesday.</p><p>Talking to Insider Wednesday, Wyatt expressed her support for President-elect Joe Biden, who was recently projected the winner of the presidential election, though Trump is disputing the results.</p><p>He has not served in the military either, but he is a Blue Star family member. His son Beau Biden served as a member of the National Guard and deployed to Iraq. Beau died of brain cancer in 2015.</p><p>\"Family members of those who are serving are an integral part of the military,\" she said. \"Although President-elect Joe Biden has never served in the military, the fact that his son did is incredibly important because at least then he understands.\"</p><p>She explained that as a veteran, this is \"very important\" to her. \"Instead of saying, 'Imagine it was your son,' he knows because it was his son,\" Wyatt said. \"He knows the cost. He understands the fear that every parent has when their child says I'm joining the military.\"</p><p>The president-elect tweeted to veterans Wednesday that he will be a president \"who respects your sacrifice, understands your service, and will never betray the values you fought so bravely to defend.\"</p><blockquote class=\"twitter-tweet blockquote\" data-lang=\"en\" data-cards=\"\" data-conversation=\"\">&#8212;Joe Biden  (@JoeBiden) <a href=\"https://twitter.com/mims/statuses/1326557341697839106?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw\">November 11, 2020</a></blockquote><script async src=\"//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"></script><p>Further voicing her support for political change in the US, Wyatt said: \"I have worked too hard and sacrificed too much. I put my blood, sweat, and tears into this country, and I refuse to let it die.\"</p><p>\"I am in it,\" she continued, \"and I'm hoping that Joe Biden and Kamala Harris are both in it as much as I am because that's the best thing that a veteran can ask of a president and a vice-president.\"</p><p>She expressed hope that the new leadership will put effort into fixing the institutional support systems that are supposed to be in place for veterans to ensure that the country has the back of those who protect and defend it, among other broken systems.</p><p>\"What I'm asking for and what veterans should be asking of our government and of our leaders is to put in your all.\" Wyatt added. \"If you're not putting in your all, then you shouldn't be in office.\"</p><div 12:49:39","updatedTime":"2020-11-12 12:49:39","title":"How to crop a PDF on your Windows computer without using a paid service","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-crop-a-pdf-on-windows","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac1cecb09abb0018625fcb?format=jpeg\" alt=\"woman with headphones using PC desktop computer\" height=\"1250\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>It&#39;s easy to crop a PDF document on your Windows PC, even without a paid service.\n<p class=\"copyright\">JGI/Jamie Grill/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>You can crop a PDF on Windows for free without having to purchase Adobe Acrobat or a similar paid service.</li>\n<li>Windows has a built-in tool called the snipping tool that allows you to crop any image on your screen and save it as its own file &#8212; including PDF documents.</li>\n<li><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tech-reference\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"summary_bullets\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"0\">Visit Business Insider's Tech Reference library for more stories</a>.</strong></li>\n</ul><p>The <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/category/pdf\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">PDF</a> format is a great way to save documents with the formatting and text locked in place — but the fact that you can't alter the text doesn't mean you can't alter other things about the document.</p><p>If you ever need to crop a PDF for any reason — say, for example, you need the text part of the document without the signatures, or you need to send one specific clause to someone without sending them the whole thing.</p><p>There are a few different ways to crop a PDF on a <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/category/windows\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Windows</a> computer, but the easiest way is through the use of the snipping tool — this method doesn't require you to use any third-party websites or to convert it to a different type of document first.</p><h2><strong>How to crop a PDF on Windows without a paid service</strong></h2><p><strong>1.</strong> Open the PDF in your computer's default PDF viewer.</p><p><strong>2.</strong> Press the Windows key to open the search bar and type \"snip\" to find and open the snipping tool.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac1327b09abb0018625f83?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How_to_crop_a_PDF_on_Windows_ _1\" height=\"821\" width=\"1600\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Open the snipping tool.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Melanie Weir/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>3.</strong> In the snipping tool window, select the shape that works best for what you want to do — rectangular will probably work best under most circumstances.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac139f7f8f4200182a6413?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How_to_crop_a_PDF_on_Windows_ _2\" height=\"822\" width=\"1600\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Select the snipping shape that works best.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Melanie Weir/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>4.</strong> Once you choose a snipping shape, the page will gray out, and your cursor will turn into a crosshair selection tool. Click and drag to select the rectangular shape you want to crop from the PDF, and let go to confirm your selection.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac15c77f8f4200182a641b?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How_to_crop_a_PDF_on_Windows_ _3\" height=\"862\" width=\"1589\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Click and drag your cursor to crop the area of your choosing.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Melanie Weir/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>5.</strong> When you're finished, a window containing your cropped area will appear. In the top right corner of the window, click \"File\" and select \"Save As…\" and choose a name for your cropped image, as well as the type of file to save it as.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac16d4b09abb0018625f9e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How_to_crop_a_PDF_on_Windows_ _4\" height=\"900\" width=\"1600\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Click &#34;File&#34; and &#34;Save As...&#34; to save the image in whatever format you prefer.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Melanie Weir/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><h2><strong>How to easily combine PDFs on Windows</strong></h2><p>Sometimes, you may want to take multiple cropped PDFs and turn them into one consolidated PDF document. This sounds like a complex process, but it's actually fairly simple.</p><p><strong>1.</strong> Open File Explorer on your computer.</p><p><strong>2.</strong> Find the documents or images you wish to combine and hover over them, checking the box in the top left corner of each one you want included.</p><ul><li><strong>Note:</strong> It is easier to do this if you save them all to one folder — that way you can simply select them by clicking and dragging over them all at once.</li></ul><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac182eb09abb0018625faf?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How_to_crop_a_PDF_on_Windows_ _5\" height=\"800\" width=\"1137\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Open File Explorer and check all the items you wish to combine.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Melanie Weir/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>3.</strong> Right-click over one of the selected items, and choose \"Print\" from the dropdown menu.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac18d27f8f4200182a643b?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How_to_crop_a_PDF_on_Windows_ _6\" height=\"800\" width=\"903\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Right click the items and select &#34;Print.&#34;\n<p class=\"copyright\">Melanie Weir/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>4.</strong> A Print menu will appear. Click the field labeled \"Printer\" at the top left of the window, and select \"Microsoft Print to PDF\" from the dropdown menu.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac19be7f8f4200182a6441?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How_to_crop_a_PDF_on_Windows_ _7\" height=\"800\" width=\"1444\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Under &#34;Printer,&#34; choose &#34;Microsoft Print to PDF.&#34;\n<p class=\"copyright\">Melanie Weir/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>5.</strong> Change any of the other document settings you may desire, including size — which you can alter by changing the size of the paper you're \"printing on\" — and layout.</p><p><strong>6.</strong> When you are finished, click \"Print.\"</p><div Those complexities, coupled with the advent of better batteries, will drive investments into \"pure\" battery electric vehicles, he said.&#160;</p><p>Previous moves by GM certainly suggest a preference for going all-electric. The automaker announced it would discontinue its Volt hybrid in 2018 and <a href=\"https://www.gmsustainability.com/highlights-and-features/ev-portfolio.html\">has announced</a> that it will release 20 fully electric vehicles by 2023.&#160;</p><p>In his panel with Business Insider, Parker said that the automaker could sell a million electric vehicles in major markets globally by 2025.&#160;Last week, GM released a Hummer electric vehicle. President Trump attended the event to celebrate the 70th birthday of the U.S. Air Force.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Alex Wong/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>The Pentagon saw a string of high-level departures this week after President Trump said he \"terminated\" the defense secretary, and the administration filled a number of those voids with Trump loyalists.</li>\n<li>Some in the Department of Defense and Congress expressed concerns about those drastic moves in the immediate aftermath of Trump's electoral defeat, with one lawmaker writing in a statement that post-election \"chaos has now reached the Pentagon.\"</li>\n<li>David Lapan, a former Department of Defense spokesman with decades of military service, told Insider that the moves do not make sense and that part of the \"cause for alarm is not knowing why this is being done.\"</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Top Pentagon leadership positions are being packed with Trump loyalists for reasons that are unclear and triggering mounting concern.</p><p>President Donald Trump <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trump-has-terminated-his-secretary-of-defense-after-losing-election-2020-11\">fired Secretary of Defense Mark Esper on Monday</a>, and the very next day, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/top-pentagon-intelligence-official-resigns-amid-post-election-shake-up-2020-11\">Chief of Staff to the Secretary of Defense Jen Stewart, Under Secretary of Defense for Policy James Anderson, and Under Secretary of Defense for Intelligence and Security Joseph Kernan resigned</a>.</p><p>Chris Miller, formerly the director of the National Counterterrorism Center, replaced Esper. Anthony Tata, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/controversial-trump-ally-takes-over-top-pentagon-policy-job-report-2020-11\">a former Fox News commentator who the Trump administration sidestepped Congress to slip into the Pentagon</a>, replaced Anderson, and Kash Patel and Ezra Cohen-Watnick, both former members of the National Security Council <a href=\"https://apnews.com/article/donald-trump-army-christopher-miller-mark-esper-james-anderson-95f848b7cdaba116b7c09787edb4c839\">considered loyal to the president</a>, replaced Stewart and Kernan.</p><p>And there is speculation that more defense officials may be on their way out and that this is just the beginning — even with only 70 days until the Biden administration takes over. Trump, however, has refused to acknowledge his defeat for five days and instead baselessly claimed election fraud.</p><p>The flurry of departures apparently sent shockwaves through the Department of Defense. A <a href=\"https://edition.cnn.com/2020/11/10/politics/trump-officials-ousted-burrowing/index.html\">defense official told CNN</a> that the situation was \"unsettling,\" adding that \"these are dictator moves.\" The <a href=\"https://apnews.com/article/donald-trump-army-christopher-miller-mark-esper-james-anderson-95f848b7cdaba116b7c09787edb4c839\">Associated Press wrote</a> that \"unease was palpable inside\" the Pentagon Tuesday.</p><p>Rep. Adam Smith, a Washington Democrat and chairman of the House Armed Services Committee, <a href=\"https://adamsmith.house.gov/press-releases?ID=92AFFFC4-9D4A-47F2-A55C-1B88642A6DCC\">sounded the alarm Tuesday afternoon</a>, accusing Trump of sowing chaos and division after losing the election. \"That chaos has now reached the Pentagon,\" he wrote.</p><p>\"I've been shot at a lot. I've been nearly killed a bunch of times. I'm not an alarmist. I try to stay cool under pressure. Mark me down as alarmed,\" <a href=\"https://www.msnbc.com/deadline-white-house/watch/gen-barry-mccaffrey-on-shakeup-at-the-pentagon-mark-me-down-as-alarmed-95737413944\">retired four-star Gen. Barry McCaffrey said on MSNBC Wednesday</a>.</p><p>\"We are watching the setup of people who are unqualified for office to be in control of the 2.1 million men and women of the armed forces,\" he added.</p><p>David Lapan, a former Pentagon spokesman with decades of military service, told Insider that part of the \"cause for alarm is not knowing why this is being done.\"</p><p>\"You have an administration with very little credibility, little to none. The level of trust is very low, so people are naturally going to think the worst,\" he added. \"And the administration isn't taking steps to reassure anyone about why they're taking these actions.\"</p><p>\"I think what has everybody most concerned is that it doesn't make sense,\" Lapan said.</p><p>If it were vindictive, a response to Trump's souring on Esper as the defense secretary, then he could have simply fired Esper and elevated Deputy Secretary of Defense David Norquist. But that didn't happen. Instead, someone was brought in from outside, and then the departures accelerated.</p><p>\"There is no rational explanation for it,\" he said. \"There are any number of bad scenarios that could play out. We don't know which of those might be true, if any, but in the absence of any better explanation, people are concerned.\"</p><p>Lapan noted that the people coming in largely appear to be unqualified or underqualified for the positions they are taking over, potentially crippling the military's leadership. Some worry these acting officials do not have the leverage to block or would even enable the orders of a president who increasingly shows little regard for democratic processes.</p><p>Their lack of experience with their new Pentagon roles also potentially hinders the transition process because when President-elect Joe Biden's team is finally able to get that process moving, they will be forced to rely on people who have only been on the job a matter of weeks.</p><p>Trump continues to contest the election and repeatedly claim Biden's win is fraudulent without evidence.</p><p>\"Again, you have an administration that operates with a deficit of trust, so in this environment, people are going to question their motives,\" Lapan said. \"People are going to worry about what could happen.\"</p><p>The problem is that the upheavals at the Pentagon create uncertainty for the Department of Defense as a whole, for both the military and civilian employees, he explained. Furthermore, it confuses America's allies, and potentially gives an opening to US adversaries.</p><p>\"All of those things are essentially damaging, not only to the Department of Defense, but to our country,\" Lapan said. \"That's why people are worked up about it. There's just a lot of potential danger there.\"</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a Pickrell)","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://i.insider.com/5ce8cb4511e20509632e9252?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx3/cdn80@2020_1/2020/11/12/04-50-03-313_2f09305ec16394f5.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn11@2020_1/2020/11/12/04-50-05-069_cc3ef43fc8ff5801.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=CdduTbFFjIQ:7zPrbiPRH_s:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn39@2020_3/2020/11/12/04-49-58-806_5cc86db952a4d58d.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=CdduTbFFjIQ:7zPrbiPRH_s:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn64@2020_6/2020/11/12/04-50-07-292_c3cc97546e2c4e32.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn48@2020_5/2020/11/12/04-49-59-767_740defb435ea442b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=CdduTbFFjIQ:7zPrbiPRH_s:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn11@2020_3/2020/11/12/04-49-58-325_9bc227d6f70ae957.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/CdduTbFFjIQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn79@2020_1/2020/11/12/04-49-55-409_ea08dda72176378d.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1605156579244},{"createdTime":"2020-11-12 12:49:39","updatedTime":"2020-11-12 12:49:39","title":"Here's what makes the Navy's 'SEAL Taxi Service' so lethal","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/what-makes-navy-special-warfare-combatant-craft-crews-so-lethal-2020-11","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac4393b09abb0018626108?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Naval Special Warfare combatant craft SWCC\" height=\"1249\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>US Navy Special Warfare Combatant-Craft Crewmen prepare for a live-fire exercise in the Aegean Sea, July 16, 2020.\n<p class=\"copyright\">US Navy/Sgt. Aven Santiago</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>The Navy's Special Warfare Combatant-Craft Crewmen don't get much attention beyond their role in ferrying Navy SEALs to and from missions.</li>\n<li>But SWCC are a small and elite group of warriors who don't get nearly enough credit for their contribution to American security.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Special Warfare Combatant-Craft Crewman, the \"Boat Guys\" in all those Navy SEALs photos, are a small and elite bunch of warriors who don't get nearly enough credit for their contribution to American security.</p><p>Here's what makes the \"SEALs Taxi Service\" so lethal.</p><p>First, yes, they have SEALs on the boats. When your payload is Navy SEALs, that's a pretty big plus in the lethality department. But SWCCs don't just drop off and pick up SEALs. They&#160;<a href=\"https://www.navy.com/careers/special-operations/swcc#ft-key-responsibilities\">also conduct their own missions</a>.</p><p>Combatant-craft crews can be sent against enemy shipping and other water traffic to shut down commerce or supply operations.</p><p>The SWCC crews keep an eye out for enemy movements or other activity in their domain. If they identify a threat, they can prosecute it themselves or report it up to the deepwater guys for help.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f44338689aff80028ab7a6c?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Naval Special Warfare combatant craft SWCC\" height=\"1200\" width=\"2063\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A Mark-V special operations craft piloted by special warfare combatant-craft crewmen off of Naval Amphibious Base Little Creek during a demonstration, July 19, 2008\n<p class=\"copyright\">US Navy/Ensign Robyn Gerstenslager</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>The SWCCs do all of this from some of the world's most advanced and dangerous small crafts.</p><p>Their boats are typically well-armed, and SWCCs train extensively on small craft tactics and strategies. The Navy prefers to deploy SWCC craft in groups so boats can provide fire support to one another. But even a single boat brings a lot of firepower.</p><p>Navy SWCCs can launch and recover their vehicles in the well decks of larger ships. And some of the boats can even be airdropped into the water for operations. All&#160;<a href=\"http://www.sealswcc.com/navy-swcc-training-stages.html\">SWCC operators are static-line parachute qualified</a>&#160;so they can jump with their boats.</p><p>Of course, jumping after a boat means the operators will land in the water. So they conduct open water swims, sometimes into near-freezing water, to prepare.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f44338c42f43f001ddfec42?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Naval Special Warfare combatant craft SWCC CH-47 helicopter\" height=\"1500\" width=\"2100\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>An Army CH-47 helicopter lifts a Naval Special Warfare 11-meter rigid-hull inflatable boat during an exercise, July 16, 2008.\n<p class=\"copyright\">US Navy/Ensign Robyn Gerstenslager</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>The Navy gets sailors ready for this grueling job by demanding constant and rigorous physical training. Navy SWCC and SEAL candidates awaiting training are assigned to the Fleet Transition Program to ensure they remain physically capable of becoming elite maritime warriors.</p><p>The&#160;<a href=\"http://www.sealswcc.com/navy-swcc-training-stages.html\">SWCC training pipeline consists four phases</a>, the two-month Naval Special Warfare Preparatory School, Naval Special Warfare Orientation, Basic Crewman Training, and Crewman Qualification Training.</p><p>And the Navy isn't afraid to recruit potential candidates while they're still young. Scout teams go into the community to seek out talented individuals who might be interested in a special operations career.</p><p>The Navy has over&#160;<a href=\"https://navyseals.com/ns-overview/navy-swcc-the-navys-elite-boat-warriors/\">700 sailors trained and assigned as SWCCs at a time</a>. This tiny force conducts dangerous and essential missions all over the world.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a 12:49:39","updatedTime":"2020-11-12 12:49:39","title":"Former Trump official was 'duped' into thanking a war criminal on Veterans Day","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/richard-grenell-duped-war-criminal-bill-calley-2020-11","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac84d27f8f4200182a66e4?format=jpeg\" alt=\"US diplomat Richard Grenell\" height=\"600\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Richard Grenell, the former acting Director of National Intelligence.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Sven Hoppe/picture alliance via Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Richard Grenell, the former acting Director of National Intelligence, was \"duped\" by a political correspondent.</li>\n<li>Ken Klippenstein, a correspondent for The Nation, asked Grenell for a shout-out for his grandfather on Twitter and misleadingly attached a photo of Bill Calley.</li>\n<li>Calley is a convicted war criminal.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Richard Grenell, the former acting Director of National Intelligence in the Trump administration, was \"duped\" after a correspondent from a left-leaning magazine fooled him into thanking a convicted war criminal for his service in the US Army.</p><p>Ken Klippenstein, a correspondent for The Nation, in a <a href=\"https://twitter.com/kenklippenstein/status/1326660240713142272?s=20\">tweet</a> attached a photo of <a href=\"https://www.washingtonpost.com/history/2019/05/25/he-was-americas-most-notorious-war-criminal-nixon-helped-him-anyway/\">Bill Calley</a> and misleadingly suggested it was his grandfather.</p><p>Calley was convicted of killing at least 22 unarmed people in the My Lai Massacre in 1968, during the Vietnam War. The Army officer was sentenced to life in prison, but after a new trial served just three years in house arrest.</p><p>Klippenstein, who is most known for his time spent online and his proficiency in submitting Freedom of Information Act requests to federal agencies, said in his tweet that his grandfather was a \"huge fan\" and that it would \"make his day\" if Grenell would give him a shout-out.</p><p>According to a screenshot of Klippenstein's direct-messages, Grenell asked him what his grandfather's name was, to which the correspondent replied by providing Calley's name.</p><p>Four minutes later, Grenell said in a tweet: \"Thank you for your service, Bill Calley!\"</p><p>Klippenstein also appeared to have sent the same message to former CIA director Michael Hayden, an official during George W. Bush and Barack Obama's tenure. Hayden <a href=\"https://twitter.com/GenMhayden/status/1326664009681166336?s=20\">tweeted</a> that he received the same message and that he knew \"exactly what was happening.\"</p><p>\"Grenell surely didn't,\" Hayden said. \"He's an asshole. Again and again.\"</p><p>Hayden, who is an outspoken critic of the Trump administration, asked Klippenstein what he did to deserve the online trolling.</p><p>Klippenstein replied by saying he \"had to uphold the spirit of bipartisanship.\"</p><p>Grenell admitted he was \"duped,\" but that in light of Veteran Day on Wednesday Klippenstein's joke was done in poor taste.</p><p>\"Duped. Trying to be helpful to people who reach out on Veteran's Day,\" Grenell <a href=\"https://twitter.com/RichardGrenell/status/1326657546975768576?s=20\">tweeted</a>. \"It's a shame people would do this on a day like today. DC is a sick city.\"</p><p>Grenell served in the Trump administration as the US ambassador to Germany before being tapped as acting DNI, replacing his predecessor, acting director Joseph Maguire. Grenell was replaced with Republican Rep. John Ratcliffe, another staunch loyalist.&#160;</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a Take this seriously.\"</p><p>Public health experts have warned that the US could see the \"deadliest\" wave yet this winter, especially if measures aren't implemented to help curb the spread.&#160;</p><p>Within the past week, the US has continued to break daily new case records. 61,964.</p><p>The US has already surpassed more than 10.3 million cases and over 240,000 deaths.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a
