Sticky</bi-shortcode><p>The flagship launch title for the PlayStation 5, \"<a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1723489852019026143\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Marvel's Spider-Man: Miles Morales</a>,\" is an impressive evolution of the bestselling PS4 game, and a wonderful demonstration of how the PS5's next-gen hardware will benefit major releases in the years to come.</p><p>In 2011, Miles Morales debuted in Marvel's \"Ultimate Comics'' line as an Afro-Latino replacement to that universe's Spider-Man. In less than 10 years, the character has become a core part of the Marvel Universe, starring in the 2019 Academy Award winner for Best Animated Feature, \"Spider-Man: Into the Spider-Verse.\"&#160;</p><p>With new powers, a different origin story, and a healthy respect for the original hero, Miles and \"Into the Spider-Verse\" helped Spider-Man evolve for a new generation of fans. As the headliner of a premier launch title, \"Marvel's Spider-Man: Miles Morales\" is designed to show players how their games will evolve in the coming generation too.</p><p>\"<a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1723489852019026143\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Marvel's Spider-Man: Miles Morales</a>\" will be released on November 12 alongside a remastered version of \" Marvel's Spider-Man\" for PlayStation 5. The game costs <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1723489852019026143\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">$50 on its own</a>, or <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1723489334156344774\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">$70 with the remaster</a>. \"Miles Morales\" is also available on <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1723489745661107141\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">PlayStation 4 for $50</a>, and there will be a paid upgrade option if you decide to buy a PS5 later.</p><h2>'Spider-Man: Miles Morales' review: A showcase for the PlayStation 5's next-gen performance</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac2f417f8f4200182a64eb?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Marvel&#39;s Spider-Man: Miles Morales PS5\" height=\"1080\" width=\"1920\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">&#34;Marvel&#39;s Spider-Man: Miles Morales&#34; / Sony</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>\"Marvel's Spider-Man\" is the bestselling PS4 game of all-time, so there's a good chance that most PlayStation fans and PS5 early adopters are familiar with the original game. <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1723489852019026143\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">\"Miles Morales\"</a> demonstrates just how the next-gen PS5 hardware can improve a game's performance with upgrades that go beyond graphics alone.</p><p>The visual improvements are immediately noticeable, with the PlayStation 5 delivering a higher resolution, new lighting and reflection effects, and a higher, more stable frame rate. Loading times improve greatly with the PlayStation 5's solid state drive — 30 to 60 second wait times from the PlayStation 4 \"Spider-Man\" are cut down to under five seconds in <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1723489852019026143\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">\"Miles Morales.\"</a></p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5b967c7f8905f2fd1e8b4f25?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Spider Man ps4\" height=\"1035\" width=\"1834\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>These subway loading screens were fun on PS4, but PS5 loads so fast you can skip them entirely.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Marvel&#39;s Spider Man</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>PlayStation 5's power boost delivers tons of small enhancements to \"Spider-Man\" too; you'll find the streets of New York bustling with more cars and people, Spider-Man can swing through the city even faster because the streets take less time to load, and the environments show sharper detail in general. Overall, \"<a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1723489852019026143\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Marvel's Spider-Man: Miles Morales</a>\" showcases how PS5 can render a beautiful, busy, open world at 4K without hiccups.</p><h2>Graphics</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac29ebb09abb001862603c?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Spider-Man Miles Morales PS5\" height=\"1406\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">&#34;Marvel&#39;s Spider-Man: Miles Morales&#34; / Sony</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1723489852019026143\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">\"Miles Morales\"</a> might be the best looking game we see during this initial run of PlayStation 5 and Xbox Series X launch titles, thanks to its expert implementation of real-time ray tracing; a premium graphics feature that's meant to be one of the PlayStation 5's hallmarks.</p><p>Ray tracing allows objects within the game world to create their own lighting effects, leading to more realistic looking shadows, reflections, and color shading. For \"<a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1723489852019026143\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Spider-Man: Miles Morales</a>,\" this means that Miles's bio-electric powers, the reflective glass covering New York's skyscrapers, and the glowing neon billboards of Times Square all create their own unique lighting effects while you play.</p><p>Ray tracing is taxing on the PS5, however, slowing the game's animations down to 30 frames per second when the graphics are set to fidelity mode. In performance mode, \"<a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1723489852019026143\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Miles Morales</a>\" runs at a full 60 frames per second, and the image quality is just slightly below 4K, though few people would notice at a glance. Performance mode does disable ray tracing effects, though.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac2d9b7f8f4200182a64e1?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Spider-Man Miles Morales PS5\" height=\"843\" width=\"1125\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Ray tracing creates some pretty awesome reflections and lighting effects.\n<p class=\"copyright\">&#34;Marvel&#39;s Spider-Man: Miles Morales&#34; / Sony</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Personally, I find myself switching back and forth between fidelity and performance mode based on whether I'm checking out story missions and cutscenes, or just casually fighting crime and exploring. Ultimately, I feel like ray tracing gives the game a wonderful level of depth, so I'd recommend using fidelity mode to start and switching later if you want a smoother experience.</p><p>The game's character models are also tremendously detailed, with facial motion capture helping characters communicate with feeling during cutscenes. If you've played the original \"Marvel's Spider-Man\" you'll notice that character faces are a bit more detailed, and Peter Parker has a whole new actor.</p><h2>Story</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac2b7fb09abb0018626049?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Spider-Man Miles Morales PS5\" height=\"844\" width=\"1500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">&#34;Marvel&#39;s Spider-Man: Miles Morales&#34; / Sony</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>\"<a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1723489852019026143\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Miles Morales</a>\" is set shortly after the events of \"Marvel's Spider-Man,\" continuing the story with a teenage Miles stepping into his first days as Spider-Man. The story lasts about eight to 10 hours with cinematic cutscenes, making it about half as long as the first game. As someone who felt like \"Marvel's Spider-Man\" should've been a bit shorter, I find Miles to be a much tighter experience.</p><p>Though Peter Parker makes an appearance early on, Miles is left to defend the city on his own after a few quick lessons and training exercises. As a young hero, Miles has to learn to fully control his powers and strike a balance between his new found responsibilities and his personal life.</p><p>A growing clash between the Roxxon Corporation and the Underground, a street gang with futuristic weapons, forces Miles to intervene as Spider-Man to prevent New York from being destroyed. He battles supervillains, like the Rhino, the Prowler, and a new version of the Tinkerer, as he fights to protect the city.</p><p>The story in \"<a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1723489852019026143\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Miles Morales</a>\" succeeds in separating the hero from Peter Parker; making him independent by highlighting his identity as an Afro-Latino New Yorker and focusing on the relationships that make him different from the original \"Spider-Man.\" There are still plenty of superhero cliches to be found in the world of \"Marvel's Spider-Man,\" but this version of Miles feels like one of his most satisfying incarnations to date.</p><h2>Gameplay</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f6e3e34a5fb5800198b2f64?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Marvel&#39;s Spider-Man: Miles Morales\" height=\"1125\" width=\"2000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Sony</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>\"<a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1723489852019026143\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Miles Morales</a>\" doesn't do much to change the basic formula of \"Marvel's Spider-Man,\" adopting the same open-world gameplay based in New York City. The map has been slightly expanded to include Miles' hometown of Harlem, and weather effects, like snow and rain, add lovely detail to familiar scenery.</p><p>Between story beats, Miles will find different crimes and neighborhood missions spread across the city. Combat is a mix of basic button presses with timed dodges and gadgets for extra flair. Miles' cloaking ability also adds an extra layer to stealth sequences. As you progress through the story, you'll unlock more moves and tools to use in fights.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac31f0b09abb0018626072?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Spider-Man Miles Morales ps5\" height=\"844\" width=\"1500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Unlike Peter Parker, Miles can make himself invisible for brief periods.\n<p class=\"copyright\">&#34;Marvel&#39;s Spider-Man: Miles Morales&#34; / Sony</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>In contrast to the car chases and shoot-outs Miles encounters, the neighborhood missions bring context and character to Miles' adventure. Answering requests on the Friendly Neighborhood Spider-Man app leads to Miles tracking a bodega cat, helping subway workers, and other complex side activities with fun rewards. Exploration is also essential, with hidden collectibles calling attention to the tremendous amount of detail within the city landscape.</p><p>The game has multiple difficulty settings and plenty of accessibility options to make sure that anyone can have fun, regardless of their age or prior experience with video games. Having completed \"Marvel's Spider-Man\" on advanced difficulty levels, I hopped into \"Miles Morales\" at the harder than normal \"Spectacular\" difficulty without issue, and I'm looking forward to starting a New Game+ on \"Ultimate\" difficulty — but not until I complete the PS5 remaster of \"Marvel's Spider-Man.\"</p><h2>Should you buy the Ultimate Edition?</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac29f0b09abb0018626040?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Spider-Man Miles Morales PS5\" height=\"1406\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">&#34;Marvel&#39;s Spider-Man: Miles Morales&#34; / Sony</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Buying the <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1723489334156344774\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">ultimate edition of \"Marvel's Spider-Man: Miles Morales\"</a> is the only way to get the remastered PS5 version of \"Marvel's Spider-Man\" right now. That $70 version will also give you access to the game on both PS4 and PS5, if you want to play \"Miles Morales\" on PS4 first and upgrade later. The <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1723489852019026143\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">standard version of \"Marvel's Spider-Man: Miles Morales\"</a> costs $50.</p><p>In my mind, the ultimate is the better choice, since the remaster of the first \"Spider-Man\" will provide dozens of hours of extra gameplay and a visual overhaul of an all-time classic game for about $20 more. If you're planning on buying the <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1723491528040262749\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">$50 PlayStation 4 version of \"Spider-Man: Miles Morales,\"</a>&#160;Sony has promised an upgrade option for gamers who buy the PlayStation 5 later on, though the price isn't known just yet.</p><h2>The bottom line</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac29efb09abb001862603f?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Spider-Man Miles Morales PS5\" height=\"1406\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">&#34;Marvel&#39;s Spider-Man: Miles Morales&#34; / Sony</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1723489334156344774\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">\"Marvel's Spider-Man: Miles Morales\"</a> is a must-have game for all PlayStation 5 owners, and I would say that includes the remaster of \"Marvel's Spider-Man,\" since the PS4 version won't look nearly as good on PS5.</p><p>As a comic book fan, longtime Spider-Man fan, and black person living near New York City, it's lovely to see Miles get the space to shine in his own game, and to see such care given to recreating the diverse neighborhood that gave birth to such a fun character.</p><p>If you haven't been able to find a PS5 yet, you might be disappointed to pay $50 for an experience that isn't nearly as optimized as the PS5 version of \"Spider-Man.\" However, the story and gameplay additions that \"Miles Morales\" brings to the table absolutely warrant the $50 Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul><li><strong>Bridgewater's Bob Prince told CNBC on Wednesday that the stock market is facing an \"overflowing river of liquidity\" from the combination of government spending to replace lost income and high rates of saving.&#160;</strong></li><li><strong>The hedge fund's co-chief investment officer said the US administration post election will only \"re-route\" the river and the liquidity is unlikely to go away with a Biden presidency.</strong></li><li><strong>However, the benefits of the liquidity don't affect all assets equally, he spending, and the new government administration will only \"reroute\" the river as there's no sign of fiscal or monetary tightening any time soon, Bob Prince <a href=\"https://www.cnbc.com/video/2020/11/11/markets-face-overflowing-river-of-liquidity-says-bridgewaters-bob-prince.html\">told CNBC on Wednesday.</a></p><p>The Bridgewater Associates co-chief investment officer said spending as a result of the pandemic is driving markets, and this is unlikely to change drastically now that the election is over. He said three kinds of financial resources are behind the spending: money, credit, and income.&#160;</p><p>\"There's lots of money out there, there's lots of credit, mostly coming from the government,\" said Prince. <br>That government borrowing has more than replaced the lost income that people have had, while savings rates have gone up.\"&#160;</p><p>This combination of replaced lost income and savings rates has produced an \"unprecedented\" accumulation of cash on balance sheets around the world, he added.&#160;</p><p><em><strong>Read more: </strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/stock-picks-to-buy-13-cheap-companies-stable-predictable-growth-2020-11?r=gr-sub\" data-analytics-position=\"7\" data-analytics-module=\"\">Buy these 13 stocks that offer stable and predictable growth without the excessive valuations of big tech, Credit Suisse says</a></em></p><p>\"There's a huge pile of money sitting out there as the inertia of the prior polices, and there's really no sign of tightening on the horizon,\" said Prince. He also said the US won't see fiscal or monetary tightening any time soon, and there's going to be more stimulus.&#160;</p><p>All of this is creating liquidity that's unlikely to change with a Biden presidency.&#160;</p><p>\"The effect of a shift in politics is somewhat of a rerouting of that river, but it's a big river that's overflowing at the banks.\"</p><p>He added that the way the coronavirus affects spending and liquidity will continue to be a \"pressure\" that adversely affects certain assets while benefiting others.&#160;&#160;</p><p>\"You have storeholds of wealth whether they be equities or gold that benefit from the liquidity effect and you have other types of assets that are hurt by the contraction and incomes and so until the virus effect on spending goes away that src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e68eab1235c180f7b1dffc4?format=jpeg\" alt=\"royal caribbean ship\" height=\"2749\" width=\"4167\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The Royal Caribbean Freedom of the Seas docked in Miami in 2008.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Lynne Sladky/AP</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>The US Center for for Disease Control and Prevention lifted its no-sail order on November 1, and Royal Caribbean will be looking for volunteers to embark on trial cruises.</li>\n<li>These cruises are a way to test safety guidelines the CDC has put in place to allow ships to set sail again.&#160;</li>\n<li>Most cruise ships have been at dock since March, when the coronavirus pandemic halted all travel.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Royal Caribbean is going to be looking for volunteers to experience the new style of cruising necessitated by pandemic-era restrictions, <a href=\"https://www.travelandleisure.com/cruises/royal-caribbean-volunteers-testing-safety-protocol\">according to Travel + Leisure.</a></p><p>The US Center for Disease Control and Prevention <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/cdc-lifts-cruising-no-sail-order-november-issues-conditions-2020-10\">officially lifted its no-sail order on November 1</a> after halting all cruises in March. But cruise ships won't be able to return to normal, as the no-sail order has been replaced with the CDC's \"Framework for Conditional Sailing Order,\" which \"introduces a phased approach for the safe and responsible resumption of passenger cruises.\"</p><p>While the cruises won't set sail until 2021, Royal Caribbean is already preparing for these trial cruises.</p><p>Those who volunteer to embark on the ships will not be paid.</p><p>\"While we are eager to welcome our guests back on board, we have a lot to do between now and then, and we're committed to taking the time to do things right,\" a Royal Caribbean spokesperson told Travel + Leisure. \"This includes training our crew in new health and safety protocols and conducting a number of trial sailings to stress-test those protocols in real-world conditions.\"</p><p>The initial cruises will likely be to Royal Caribbean's private island, CocoCay, Vicki Freed, the senior vice president of sales, trade support, and service said <a href=\"https://www.cruiseindustrynews.com/cruise-news/23817-royal-caribbean-may-need-volunteers-for-trial-cruises.html\">during an interview with Cruise Industry News earlier this month.</a> The location would offer isolation from outsiders, acting as its own bubble.</p><p>\"It is going to require a lot of work to restart operations,\" Freed said. \"It is complicated to go through this entire CDC recommendation and we are going to do it.\"</p><p>This news comes after cruise lines joined together <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/norwegian-royal-caribbean-create-coronavirus-covid-19-safety-panel-cruise-2020-7\">earlier this year to create the Healthy Sail Panel,</a> which was a set of guidelines the companies had proposed in order to set sail again.&#160;</p><p>Like other travel-based industries, cruise companies saw business crater amid the pandemic. Most are based overseas, and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/cruise-lines-battered-by-coronavirus-could-be-left-out-bailout-2020-3\">did not receive government money to help them stay afloat.</a></p><p>At publication time, Royal Caribbean did not respond to requests for comment.&#160;</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a Smith)","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://i.insider.com/5e68eab1235c180f7b1dffc4?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn47@2020_2/2020/11/12/04-50-03-236_6a8d30cb9d5a214d.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn11@2020_1/2020/11/12/04-50-05-069_cc3ef43fc8ff5801.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=UMTPtwY2LEc:WCjVn3Q6Ofo:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn47@2020_6/2020/11/12/04-49-57-082_3a53f567007d2cdf.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=UMTPtwY2LEc:WCjVn3Q6Ofo:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn72@2020_1/2020/11/12/04-50-02-040_efee476dbd29c98c.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn48@2020_5/2020/11/12/04-49-59-767_740defb435ea442b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=UMTPtwY2LEc:WCjVn3Q6Ofo:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn43@2020_5/2020/11/12/04-50-07-211_b8fcec21d93c0159.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/UMTPtwY2LEc":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn56@2020_3/2020/11/12/04-49-55-121_e359e02717efa1af.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1605156579278},{"createdTime":"2020-11-12 12:49:39","updatedTime":"2020-11-12 12:49:39","title":"Americans are more likely to be struck by lightning than commit election fraud","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/voter-election-fraud-statistics-rare-president-biden-trump-2020-2020-11","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac135fb09abb0018625f86?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Vote counting \" height=\"1000\" width=\"2000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Ballots are counted at the Allegheny County Election Division warehouse on the Northside of Pittsburgh, Friday, Nov. 6, 2020.\n<p class=\"copyright\">AP Photo/Gene J. Puskar</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>President Trump and his allies have filed multiple unsuccessful lawsuits and are spreading misinformation in an attempt to undermine the results of the 2020 election.&#160;</li>\n<li>The campaign has not succeeded in proving the evidence of widespread fraud in court, and election officials in the majority of states confirmed the lack of fraud in their states to The New York Times.&#160;</li>\n<li>Historically, voter and election fraud has been incredibly rare and affected a tiny percentage of all votes cast in the 21st century, academic studies and journalistic reviews have found.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>President Donald Trump and his allies are refusing to recognize the results of the 2020 presidential election and seeking to undermine confidence in the results with vague, baseless claims of election fraud.</p><p>Insider and Decision Desk HQ projected on Friday, November 6, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/joe-biden-wins-general-election-against-donald-trump-2020-11\">that President-elect Joe Biden had won Pennsylvania's 20 Electoral College votes</a>, and with them, the presidency.&#160;</p><p>Biden currently leads in the three swing states of Michigan, Pennsylvania, and Wisconsin by over 215,000 combined votes compared to the 77,744 votes by which Trump <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/elections/2016/results/president\">carried those three states combined in 2016.</a> It would be practically impossible for Trump to win those states through legal challenges or recounts.&#160;</p><p>As Insider's Jacob Shamsian has reported, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trump-lawsuits-lack-voter-fraud-claims-2020-11\">the Trump campaign itself has failed to produce any credible evidence of serious voter fraud</a> in either courts of law or in the court of public opinion, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trump-campaign-lawsuits-election-results-2020-11\">with judges ruling against the campaign</a> in all 12 of the suits they have filed in states including Georgia, Michigan, Nevada, and Pennsylvania.&#160;</p><p><a href=\"https://twitter.com/bradheath/status/1326347647154794496\">A Trump campaign lawyer admitted that the campaign was not claiming the presence of massive fraud</a> in a recent hearing for a lawsuit challenging mail ballot counting procedures in Montgomery County, Pennsylvania. And in another legal challenge, the Trump campaign raised questionable claims of fraud <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trump-pennsylvania-election-lawsuit-allege-voter-fraud-2-counties-2020-11\">in two counties that Trump had decisively won.&#160;</a></p><p>Outside of the courtroom, many of Trump's powerful allies in elected office or in conservative media have failed to substantiate their allegations of sweeping voter fraud or election irregularities, or presented questionable evidence that has since fallen apart under scrutiny, as comprehensive fact-checking claims <a href=\"https://www.buzzfeednews.com/article/janelytvynenko/post-elections-debunks?utm_source=dynamic&utm_campaign=bftwbuzzfeedpol&ref=bftwbuzzfeedpolzfeedpol\">from journalists at Buzzfeed News</a> from <a href=\"https://twitter.com/Ike_Saul/status/1324435797374808066\">A Plus' Isaac Saul has shown.&#160;</a></p><p>Election officials in 45 states also recently confirmed to The New York Times <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/2020/11/10/us/politics/voting-fraud.html\">that they are seeing no evidence of fraud in their states</a>, and a group of 28 international election observers who observed voting in multiple states <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/international-observers-say-no-voter-fraud-us-election-oas-2020-11\">said in a preliminary report</a> that they witnessed a remarkably well-run election with no evidence of fraud or malfeasance.&#160;</p><h2>An American is more likely to be struck by lightning than to commit election fraud</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac3b857f8f4200182a654d?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Voting booths\" height=\"1000\" width=\"2000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Table top voting booths are stored at the Allegheny County Election Division warehouse on the Northside of Pittsburgh, Friday, Nov. 6, 2020.\n<p class=\"copyright\">AP Photo/Gene J. Puskar</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>While fraud or attempts at fraud happens on a very small scale in every national election, it's incredibly rare and affects a minuscule percentage of all ballots cast. And partly because election administration in the United States is decentralized down to the local level, it never occurs at a rate that would change the outcome of an election.</p><p>A comprehensive but nonexhaustive database of voter and election fraud cases <a href=\"https://www.heritage.org/voterfraud/\">maintained by the conservative Heritage Foundation</a> finds documented cases of fraud with mail ballots are more common than cases of in-person voter impersonation, ballot petition fraud, and registration fraud, but that <strong>overall rates of fraud are infinitesimally low.&#160;</strong></p><p>Heritage's database identified 193 criminal convictions, civil penalties, diversions, or other official findings for fraudulent use of mail ballots between 2000 and 2020, a time period during which approximately 250 million mail ballots were cast.</p><p>As MIT elections scholar Charles Stewart and National Vote At Home Institute CEO Amber McReynolds <a href=\"https://thehill.com/opinion/campaign/494189-lets-put-the-vote-by-mail-fraud-myth-to-rest\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"40\" data-uri=\"0e38a9996800df757ae9c349d3691325\">noted in an April op-ed</a>, that puts the rate of mail ballots resulting in criminal convictions at 0.0006% and the rate of mail ballots resulting in any kind of official action at 0.00007%.&#160;</p><p>Rates of fraud are also extremely low in states that send all voters ballots. <a href=\"https://www.heritage.org/voterfraud/search\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"40\" data-uri=\"8d3698e4b182e9bf0235f39ba2ab9b95\">Heritage's database</a>&#160;reports two documented cases of fraudulent use of mail ballots in Oregon, five in Colorado, six in Washington, and none in Hawaii or Utah over the past fifteen years.&#160;</p><p>A 2012 <a href=\"https://votingrights.news21.com/interactive/election-fraud-database/\">News21 journalism investigation</a> identified just 2,068 potential cases of voter and election fraud and 491 potential cases of mail ballot fraud between 2000 and 2012, out of hundreds of millions of cast ballots.&#160;</p><p><a href=\"https://www.heritage.org/voterfraud/search?combine=&state=All&year=&case_type=All&fraud_type=24493fraud_type=24493\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\" data-uri=\"e043bdade6f0584367694006c000cae2\">Heritage's database</a> has identified just 13 cases of in-person voter impersonation documented between six states over the past 16 years, and a&#160;<a href=\"https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/wonk/wp/2014/08/06/a-comprehensive-investigation-of-voter-impersonation-finds-31-credible-incidents-out-of-one-billion-ballots-cast/\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"80\" data-uri=\"5d77354b50030a27c4043ff7069bf9a3\">2014 study from Loyola University Law School professor and elections scholar Justin Levitt</a>&#160;found just 31 credible cases of voter impersonation between 2000 and 2014, a time period during which over one billion votes were cast.&#160;</p><p><a href=\"https://www.brennancenter.org/our-work/analysis-opinion/false-narrative-vote-mail-fraud\">T</a><a href=\"https://www.brennancenter.org/our-work/analysis-opinion/false-narrative-vote-mail-fraud\">he Brennan Center for Justice concludes</a> that \"it is still more likely for an American to be struck by lightning\" than to commit voter fraud either through in-person voting or with mail ballots.&#160;</p><p>Trump's claims that ballots are sent out to millions of people with no oversight or security measures are false.</p><p>Every state, and especially those that conduct their elections almost entirely by mail, <a href=\"https://www.brennancenter.org/our-work/analysis-opinion/false-narrative-vote-mail-fraud\">have multiple checks throughout the system and layers of security to ensure the integrity of each ballot</a>, which reduces the incentive to commit fraud.&#160;</p><p>These include election officials placing specific barcodes and identifying numbers on every ballot, ballot tracking systems that allow voters to track their ballot every step of the way, required signatures on every ballot and in many states, signature verification, in which a signature on a voter's ballot is cross-matched with a signature on file with their elections office.&#160;</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>President-elect Joe Biden has won Arizona, as of 10:29 p.m. ET on Wednesday with more than 99% of the state's votes counted.</li>\n<li>Arizona is normally a Republican mainstay in presidential elections. The state has voted for a Republican president in every election but one since 1972.&#160;</li>\n<li>The state's delegation in Congress is split: six Democrats and five Republicans.&#160;</li>\n<li>Arizona holds 11 electoral votes.</li>\n<li>See the live coverage and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/2020-election-results\">full results from the US presidential election.</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>As of 10:29 p.m. ET on Wednesday, President-elect Joe Biden has won the state of Arizona and its 11 electoral votes, Decision Desk HQ and Insider projected.&#160;</p><p>Maricopa County, home to more than 60% of Arizonans, has more results to report as election officials there make their way through the count. Encompassing the Phoenix area, the county has trended towards Democrats in recent years.</p><p>There are major down-ballot races in the Senate and House, including the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/arizona-1st-district-house-election-tom-ohalleran-tiffany-shedd-2020\">1st District</a>, the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/arizona-2nd-district-house-election-ann-kirkpatrick-brandon-martin-2020\">2nd District</a> in the southeast, and the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/arizona-6th-district-house-election-david-schweikert-hiral-tipirneni-2020\">6th District</a> in Phoenix's northern suburbs.</p><p>The state's congressional delegation is split: six Democrats and five Republicans in Congress. Both houses of the state legislature and the position of governor, however, are held by Republicans. Arizona has 11 electoral votes and is <a href=\"https://projects.fivethirtyeight.com/2020-election-forecast/arizona/\">believed by analysts</a> to be competitive.</p><p>Arizona, and particularly Maricopa County, has seen significant demographic shifts in recent years that have helped move the state to the left. The state has seen an influx in new residents from the coasts, people with higher educational attainment, and Latinos, who are disproportionately younger and have been activated by years of the state GOP's attacks on immigration.</p><p>Polling has also shown that Arizona's suburban women shifted leftwards this cycle. This group has been crucial to Democratic victories across the country, both this year and in 2018. The state elected its first Democratic senator in decades — Sen. Kyrsten Sinema — in 2018.</p><p>Arizona political strategists say Trump's regular attacks on former Arizona Sen. John McCain, a longserving political moderate and Vietnam veteran, has also hurt the president's popularity among establishment Republicans and independents in the state.</p><p>Arizona, which Trump won by just over three points in 2016, has voted Republican for every election but one since 1972.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a 12:49:39","updatedTime":"2020-11-12 12:49:39","title":"A Brooklyn-based lingerie brand has sued mega-influencer Danielle Bernstein and Saks, Shopbop, and Carbon 38, alleging they sold copied designs","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/the-great-eros-lawsuit-danielle-bernstein-saks-shopbop-carbon-38-2020-11","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f8ddcbac21cfb0019468d7c?format=jpeg\" alt=\"danielle bernstein\" height=\"2474\" width=\"3554\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Danielle Bernstein, popular influencer, at Paris Fashion Week in 2019.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Christian Vierig/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Danielle Bernstein is a mega-influencer whose blog-turned-fashion brand WeWoreWhat has over 2.5 million followers on Instagram.</li>\n<li>In October, Brooklyn-based lingerie company The Great Eros said WeWoreWhat copied their signature tissue paper design, and put it on swimsuits and leggings.</li>\n<li>But WeWoreWhat beat Eros to the legal punch, filing a complaint against the brand, claiming that they didn't violate Eros' intellectual property.</li>\n<li>Now, Eros is fighting back, with a lawsuit that names not only Bernstein's WeWoreWhat as a defendant, but also retailers Onia, Saks, Shopbop, and Carbon 38, who the suit alleges sold the copied designs.&#160;</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>A Brooklyn-based lingerie company is suing mega-influencer Danielle Bernstein, as well as retailers that sold her brand's apparel, alleging that they sold apparel that copied the lingerie store's designs, according to a lawsuit filed Wednesday in California.&#160;</p><p>Lingerie brand The Great Eros accused Bernstein and her label, WeWoreWhat, of copying the pattern of female nudes that adorns Eros' tissue paper, and selling swimsuits, wallpaper, and other merchandise with the stolen design. In addition, the suit names luxury retailer Saks Fifth Avenue, online retailer Shopbop, swimsuit brand Onia, and retailer Carbon 38 as defendants in the lawsuit, claiming that they sold the stolen designs.&#160;</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f8df4b49e9fe4001900a340?format=jpeg\" alt=\"the great eros bernstein designs\" height=\"868\" width=\"1116\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>On the left, the design Danielle Bernstein used for apparel and wallpaper. On the right, the tissue paper pattern used at The Great Eros&#39; store.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Filing from the US District Court, Southern District of New York</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>The legal battle between Bernstein's WeWoreWhat and The Great Eros kicked off in October, when WeWoreWhat and swimsuit brand Onia <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/weworewhat-danielle-bernstein-the-great-eros-lawsuit-nude-pattern-designs-2020-10\">filed a complaint against The Great Eros</a>, claiming that they didn't violate any intellectual properties laws and saying the design was not copied.&#160;</p><p>In a statement on social media in October, Bernstein said that her company's pattern was influenced by Matisse's line drawings, not by Eros' tissue paper. She further denied allegations of copying, saying that she hadn't even bought or been given free merchandise from the store, and that she had checked with WheWoreWhat's designers, and found that they weren't aware of Eros' pattern either.&#160;</p><p>Eros' counsel Jeff Gluck told Business Insider strongly pushed back on these claims in an interview with Business Insider in October. He said that that he had evidence, in the form of showroom logs and gifting requests, that proved that Bernstein visited Eros' showroom (not its retail store), and that Bernstein had previously requested free merchandise from The Great Eros, Gluck said.</p><p>Gluck also clarified that in terms of intellectual property, Eros wasn't claiming that they owned the rights to line drawings of female nudes. He said that the design similarities between Eros' tissue paper and WhatWeWore's merchandise had multiple design similarities, such as the weight of the lines in the drawings and the way that the figures were arranged.&#160;</p><p>The Great Eros slammed Bernstein's decision to sue in a social media post in October.</p><p>\"Danielle, you have become a bully... You just drove 100 mph into a brick wall, because your bulls--t stops here and now,\" the brand wrote.&#160;</p><p>\"I am an advocated and committed supporter of small businesses, and as an entrepreneur and designer, I hold creative liberty and ownership in the highest regard,\" Bernstein responded on Instagram.</p><p>Saks Fifth Avenue, Onia, Bernstein, WeWoreWhat, Carbon 38, and Shopbop did not immediately respond to Business Insider's requests for comment.&#160;</p><p>WeWoreWhat has faced <a href=\"https://www.insider.com/danielle-bernstein-controversies-timeline-copying-designers-lawsuits-covid-19-2020-10\">allegations of copying smaller designers in the past</a>, including a face-mask design in July. Since starting her blog WeWoreWhat in 2011, <a href=\"https://www.insider.com/danielle-bernstein-jade-myers-poshmark-swimwear-feud-2020-1\">Bernstein has released designs</a> that include overalls, swimwear, and more. Her designs have been carried in stores ranging from Intermix to Macy's. In 2019, she launched ShopWeWoreWhat.com, an ecommerce site to sell her fashion lines.&#160;</p><p>WeWoreWhat has partnered in the past with Onia, which is also a party in the lawsuit filed by The Great Eros. The latest collaboration between the brands in May 2019 sold $1 million within three hours of its release, <a href=\"https://wwd.com/business-news/business-features/onia-danielle-bernstein-weworewhat-rakes-1-million-3-hours-1203121131/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-stringify-link=\"https://wwd.com/business-news/business-features/onia-danielle-bernstein-weworewhat-rakes-1-million-3-hours-1203121131/\" data-sk=\"tooltip_parent\">WWD reported</a>.</p><div Andrew Cuomo on Wednesday announced several new measures aimed at mitigating the spread of the novel coronavirus as cases rise in the state and across the US.</p><p>Among several changes, announced by the governor on Twitter, include a <a href=\"https://twitter.com/NYGovCuomo/status/1326596760710602753\">prohibition on gatherings in private residences that exceed 10 people</a>. The announcement comes just 15 days before Thanksgiving and goes into effect on Friday — less than two weeks from the holiday.</p><p>The office of the governor did not return Business Insider's request for comment on Wednesday about how he expected the order to be enforced.</p><p>Additionally, Cuomo announced that beginning Friday, any business with a license to sell liquor, including bars and restaurants, must close their doors no later than 10 p.m. Gyms, which <a href=\"https://www.governor.ny.gov/news/governor-cuomo-announces-gyms-and-fitness-centers-can-reopen-starting-august-24#:~:text=Cuomo%20today%20announced%20that%20gyms,to%20open%20by%20September%202.\">reopened to patrons at the end of August</a> after a monthslong closure, will remain open but also must close at 10 p.m, he said.</p><p>\"COVID is getting worse by the day,\" <a href=\"https://twitter.com/NYGovCuomo/status/1326598181904388096\">Cuomo said in a tweet</a>. \"All around the country. The fall surge is here. We are taking action but we need New Yorkers to do their part. Wear a mask. Get tested. Follow all health guidelines. Take this seriously.\"</p><p>Numerous public health experts have warned against large gatherings for the holidays, urging Americans to <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/us-coronavirus-experts-share-thanksgiving-holiday-plans-2020-10\">change or tweak their typical plans</a> to celebrate the holiday safely during the pandemic.&#160;</p><p>According to data analyzed by the <a href=\"https://coronavirus.jhu.edu/region/us/new-york\">Johns Hopkins University</a>, the state of New York has experienced at least 532,180 confirmed cases of COVID-19, resulting in more than 30,000 deaths. Most cases and deaths in the state occurred in the first months of the pandemic when New York was a global epicenter of the pandemic.</p><p>Over the past seven days, more than 2% of all COVID-19 tests You can link your <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/category/epic-games\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Epic Games</a> account to your <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/category/xbox-live\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Xbox Live</a> account as well.&#160;</p><p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/category/xbox\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Xbox</a> doesn't currently have an app for Epic Games, but you can still link the two accounts – you'll just have to do so using the desktop website instead of your Xbox console.</p><h2><strong>How to link Epic Games account to <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1723307155493771419\" rel=\"nofollow sponsored\">Xbox</a></strong></h2><p><strong>1.</strong> On a computer, go to the <a href=\"https://www.epicgames.com/store/en-US/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Epic Games website</a> and sign in to your account.&#160;</p><p><strong>2.</strong> Once you're signed in, hover your cursor over your username in the upper right corner of the screen. When the dropdown menu appears, click \"Account.\"&#160;</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fa98f5d1df1d50018219a35?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How_to_link_Epic_Games_account_to_PS4_ _2\" src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fa9900cf7d1cb0019e3a963?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How_to_link_Epic_Games_account_to_PS4_ _3\" height=\"817\" width=\"1791\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Click &#34;Connections&#34; from the menu on the left.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Chrissy Montelli/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>4.</strong> Under the Connections header, click the \"Accounts\" tab.&#160;</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fa99073f7d1cb0019e3a967?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How_to_link_Epic_Games_account_to_PS4_ _4\" height=\"822\" width=\"1748\" Treadmill</a>.&#160;</p><p>It has a 3.5-horsepower motor, which allows it to stand up to daily use, and it boasts a belt deck that measures 22 by 60 inches, which is perfect for most runners. When you're training for races with hills, you'll appreciate this treadmill's ability to reach a 15% incline and a 3% decline, which better simulates hills than most other treadmills.&#160;</p><p>The ProForm treadmill also has a number of techy features, including a 7-inch screen that's compatible with iFit workouts, a music port for iPods, and many workout apps. It also has ProShox Cushioning to lessen the impact for runners.&#160;</p><p><strong>Pros: </strong>Good motor, large running belt of 22 by 60 inches, includes both an incline and a decline setting, offers good interval training features</p><p><strong>Cons: </strong>Customer service may be disappointing if you have problems, very heavy treadmill</p>\n\tThe best treadmill for quiet workouts\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5a53c7d13225de1e008b50f3?format=jpeg\" alt=\"treadmill\" height=\"649\" width=\"865\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">3G Cardio</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>The&#160;<a href=\"https://www.3gcardio.com/shop/elite-runner-treadmill/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">3G Cardio Elite Runner Treadmill</a>&#160;delivers excellent performance and runs quieter than most treadmills.</h3><p>Few treadmills made for use at home will deliver the kind of quiet performance that the&#160;<a href=\"https://www.3gcardio.com/shop/elite-runner-treadmill/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">3G Cardio Elite Runner Treadmill</a>&#160;delivers. It's made for tall or heavy runners looking a tough workout, but you'll pay more than $3,000 for the kind of quality that this 3G Cardio unit delivers.</p><p>It has an Ortho Flex Shock suspension system to minimize the stress of impact for runners, and the 22 by 62-inch platform is perfect for running.</p><p>The 3G Cardio comes with many pre-programmed workouts and a fitness level test. You have access to speed and elevation settings, heart rate control, and workout customization.&#160; This treadmill also has a 4.0 horsepower motor and 3-inch rollers for great performance.</p><p>As you would expect with a treadmill with such a high price point, the 3G Cardio Elite consists of thick steel tubing in the frame. It's also rather expensive, so this is really only for serious runners who want a treadmill that will last a lifetime.</p><p><strong>Pros:&#160;</strong>Strong steel frame that will support a lot of weight, unit runs quieter than most treadmills, large treadmill belt area for tall runners, includes a large motor to compare favorably to gym treadmills</p><p><strong>Cons:&#160;</strong>Extremely high price point, very heavy equipment that is difficult to move around</p>\n\tThe best high-end treadmill\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e14faf4f44231418419bce5?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Peloton Tread\" height=\"461\" width=\"615\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://www.onepeloton.com/shop/tread\" target=\"_blank\">Peloton</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>The <a href=\"https://www.onepeloton.com/shop/tread-plus\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Peloton Tread+</a> has a steep price tag but offers the same high-quality daily workout classes and a deep well of content fans of its popular stationary bike have come to expect.</h3><p>Peloton's made its name by peddling (and quite literally pedaling) its popular stationary bike and companion workout classes for the last several years. With the Tread+, the company used that same tried-and-true formula to deliver a high-quality treadmill experience.&#160;</p><p>Where the Tread+ differs from traditional treadmills is both with its intuitive design and built-in display. On either arm of the unit are two dials, one to increase or decrease speed and another to increase or decrease the incline angle. Each dial turns smoothly enough that you're able to easily adjust either metric with the speed or incline quickly following suit.&#160;</p><p>Peloton's thoughtful design also extends to its low-impact slat belt that works well to absorb shock while also not being terribly loud as you run. This also means that it allows for a much smoother and comfortable run experience.</p><p>A Peloton workout unit wouldn't be complete without a massive display sitting front and center, and the Tread+ is no different, sporting a gorgeous 32-inch touchscreen monitor. The display is where the Peloton magic happens, as it's able to stream the live and pre-recorded classes, shows your in-class stats such as time and distance ran, and is your navigation tool for Peloton's content library. There's even a 20-watt built-in soundbar that flanks the bottom of the screen capable of pumping out impressive quality sound.&#160;</p><p>Then there's the price. Starting at $4,295 for the basic package, the Tread+ is no drop in the bucket. Factor in the recurring $39 subscription package for access to Peloton's content and you end up with quite the investment. Still, if you're able to afford it, the quality of the Tread, as well as the benefit of its workout and wide range of content, make it one of our favorite treadmills on the market.&#160;</p><p><strong>Pros:&#160;</strong>Intuitive design, easy-to-use speed and incline dials, beautiful 32-inch touchscreen display with built-in soundbar, and access to Peloton's deep library of workout content</p><p><strong>Cons:&#160;</strong>Expensive initial investment and recurring subscription fee</p>\n\tThe best budget treadmill\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5a53cc493225deb4198b4e5d?format=jpeg\" alt=\"treadmill\" height=\"743\" width=\"990\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Horizon Fitness</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>Compared to other budget fold-up treadmills, the <a href=\"https://go.redirectingat.com/?id=35871X943606&#38;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.horizonfitness.com%2Fhorizon-t101-treadmill\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow nofollow sponsored\">Horizon Fitness T101-04 Treadmill</a> has nice features and good performance.</h3><p>Saving space with a fold-up treadmill is a great idea for a lot of people. However, most fold-up treadmills don't offer a lot of power.</p><p>So understanding some of the natural limitations of fold-up treadmills, you'll like the <a href=\"https://go.redirectingat.com/?id=35871X943606&#38;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.horizonfitness.com%2Fhorizon-t101-treadmill\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow nofollow sponsored\">Horizon Fitness T101-04 Treadmill</a>, which works well for walkers and people on a budget. However, this model really isn't made for runners looking for high-end workouts.</p><p>It has a 55-inch belt length, a maximum 10 mph speed, and a 2.25-horsepower motor, which is good for walkers. The T101-04 treadmill is easy to fold up for storage and is a great value for those who need basic features for walking or light running.</p><p><strong>Pros: </strong>Very good price point for an entry-level treadmill, will save space with a fold-up design, runs quieter than most budget-priced treadmills, works better for walkers and light runners</p><p><strong>Cons: </strong>Only a 55-inch belt length, not really made for high-end running workouts, longevity is questionable</p>\n\tThe best shock-absorbing treadmill\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5a53cd653225de9a0a8b4f80?format=jpeg\" alt=\"treadmill\" height=\"631\" width=\"841\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">LifeSpan</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>The <a href=\"https://go.skimresources.com?id=35871X943606&#38;xs=1&#38;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.lifespanfitness.com%2Ftr3000i-folding-treadmill\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow nofollow nofollow sponsored\">LifeSpan TR3000i</a> uses an extensive shock absorption system to take some pressure off your joints while running.</h3><p>Some people dislike working out on a treadmill because of the pressure it places on their joints. The <a href=\"https://go.skimresources.com?id=35871X943606&#38;xs=1&#38;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.lifespanfitness.com%2Ftr3000i-folding-treadmill\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow nofollow nofollow sponsored\">LifeSpan TR3000i</a> attempts to alleviate some of this pressure by using a shock absorption system in the treadmill's deck.</p><p>It has a 20 x 56-inch running surface, 15 incline levels, and a 6-inch LCD screen that shows your time, calories, distance, steps, heart rate, speed, and incline.&#160;The eight shock absorber elements in the deck ensure that it's very stable and comfortable to run on.&#160;</p><p>Beyond its shock-absorbing capabilities, the TR3000i has a number of fun features to give you variety in your workouts, including a tablet holder, a USB charging port, and compatibility with iPods.</p><p><strong>Pros: </strong>Good price for a mid-range treadmill, unit folds up to save storage space, extensive shock absorption system, good feature set versus other models in this price range</p><p><strong>Cons: </strong>Not really designed for high-end workouts, build quality of treadmill is questionable</p>\n\tThe best under desk treadmill\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f5bcf3d7ed0ee001e25ee58?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Cubii1\" height=\"529\" width=\"705\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Cubii</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>The <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B01GQQ584O/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_010918_best-treadmills-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B01GQQ584O&#38;linkId=44db56423faf6cb3a96fba5e783bbe2e\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow sponsored\">Cubii Pro</a> is an easy-to-use, under desk exercise machine that's more of an elliptical than a treadmill but still allows you to log some quality cardio no matter if you're sitting down for lunch or powering through a backlog of emails.&#160;</h3><p>Though the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B01GQQ584O/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_010918_best-treadmills-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B01GQQ584O&#38;linkId=44db56423faf6cb3a96fba5e783bbe2e\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow sponsored\">Cubii Pro</a> isn't exactly a treadmill in the traditional sense (and is more of an elliptical style machine than anything else), it's unobtrusive nature makes it a convenient addition to anyone's home gym. The machine simply sits on the floor, be it under a desk, next to a coffee table, or literally anywhere around the house, and lets you pedal away for as long as you like.&#160;</p><p>The machine delivers low impact cardio that may benefit those unable to run on a treadmill due to sore joints, and it's quiet operation even allows it to be used while watching TV, talking on the phone, or listening to music. With eight different levels of resistance, it affords as easy or as difficult a workout as you like, too.&#160;</p><p>A companion smartphone application lets you keep track of all your logged workouts and lets you set weekly and monthly goals or share your progress with friends. The app is also compatible with services like Fitbit or Apple HealthKit, so if you prefer the interface of those, all workout data can easily sync to them.</p><p>At $349, it's certainly not a drop in the bucket but it is far cheaper than even the budget model on this list. For convenient, low impact cardio exercise, the Cubii Pro is as versatile and easy-to-use as it gets.&#160;</p><p><strong>Pros:&#160;</strong>Small, easy-to-use machine that delivers an effective cardio workout, has up to eight different resistance settings, offers companion app support</p><p><strong>Cons:&#160;</strong>Not strictly a treadmill, might not be as intense for hardcore fitness buffs</p><div id=\"ProductCard_5f5bd4b5bf96b946cc1be71e\" style=\"position:relative; display:block; width: 100%\"><iframe src=\"https://produktor.businessinsider.com/productCardService?id=5f5bd4b5bf96b946cc1be71e&type=small&live=true\" width=\"100%\" height=\"150%\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"\" style=\"position:absolute; top:0; left: 0\"></iframe></div><p>&#160;</p>\n\tHow to shop for a treadmill\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5a54de1dc32ae6d21a8b50e6?format=jpeg\" alt=\"treadmill running working out gym\" height=\"1334\" width=\"1778\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Scott Barbour/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>Types of treadmills</h3><p>According to <a href=\"https://www.consumerreports.org/cro/treadmills/buying-guide\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Consumer Reports</a>, treadmills fit into three basic categories based on the type of workouts they handle.</p><ul style=\"list-style-type: disc; padding-left: 30px; font-family: Georgia,Times,sans-serif;\"><li><strong>Basic: </strong>The most basic type of treadmill only works for walkers. They will have simple tracking features, such as speed, distance, and time. Most basic units will have a short bed that works better for a walker's stride than for running. And you'll find limited shock absorption features here, which isn't great for runners. Such treadmills will fold up for easy storage (although some more expensive treadmills also can fold up for storage).</li><li><strong>Mid-range: </strong>These treadmills will work for walkers or runners. For walkers, a mid-range treadmill should have longer support arms, allowing you to balance yourself easier. The belt bed will be a bit longer than the basic treadmill, but those with long running strides may still struggle. You'll see better tech features in this price range, including a heart rate monitor worn on the chest or pre-set training programs.</li><li><strong>Top-end: </strong>The highest quality of treadmills will contain long belt beds with good shock absorption, making them perfect for runners. To gain these features, such treadmills rarely will fold up for storage, meaning they require a lot of free space. They will deliver greater maximum speed levels and greater levels of incline, too. These treadmills will consist of the highest-quality materials. You'll receive Wi-Fi connectivity and extensive pre-set exercise programs with these models.</li></ul><h3>Key features of treadmills</h3><p>As treadmills evolved, companies began adding a suite of high-tech features. However, don't focus entirely on the bells and whistles of expensive treadmills. Pay attention to its physical parts, too, to find the best possible unit for your needs.</p><ul style=\"list-style-type: disc; padding-left: 30px; font-family: Georgia,Times,sans-serif;\"><li><strong>Exercise programs: </strong>Treadmills may have pre-programmed workouts that can help you with weight loss, cardiovascular performance, speed workouts, or hills training. These programs will allow you to set the length of exercise time, but they will automatically change the speed of the treadmill and the incline to match the parameters of the pre-programmed workout.</li><li><strong>Horsepower: </strong>Any treadmill motor with a continuous duty measurement of at least 2.0 should be sufficient for most people, says <a href=\"https://www.precor.com/en-us/purchase-tools/buying-guides/treadmill-buying-guide-choose-right-treadmill-you\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Precor</a>. Smaller motors will work better for walkers and larger motors work better for runners.</li><li><strong>Incline and decline: </strong>To help with training for running on hills or for additional calorie burn, the treadmill needs to offer an incline. Most treadmills can reach at least a 12% incline grade. Some treadmills even give you a simulation of running downhill with a decline grade of around 3%.</li><li><strong>Length: </strong>Runners need a treadmill belt bed of roughly 55-60 inches long, while walkers can use one closer to 45-50 inches long. Taller people will need an even longer belt bed. Remember that the length of the treadmill isn't the same as the length of the bed. The treadmill length (and width, for that matter) must accommodate the base portion of the unit that doesn't move, as well as the bed's motor housing at the front of the unit.</li><li><strong>Safety line: </strong>Treadmills will contain a safety line that hooks into the unit. You'll clip the safety line to your shirt. Should you stumble, the safety line will disconnect from the treadmill, causing it to shut down immediately. This is a nice safety feature, and it prevents those common TV and movie gags where the person using the treadmill falls and gets launched into a wall. Trust us, this gag looks funny, but it also really, really hurts, so the safety line will save you some pain.</li><li><strong>Speed: </strong>The speed with which the bed rotates on the treadmill is measured in miles per hour. Most people don't need anything over 10 mph, but those seeking heavy-duty interval workouts can find speeds up to 15 mph in a top-end treadmill.</li><li><strong>Support rails: </strong>A treadmill made for walkers, especially elderly walkers, should have long support rails on the sides that you can grip while using the treadmill to steady yourself.</li><li><strong>Touch screen controls: </strong>You should be able to adjust the incline, speed, and program in use through the touchscreen monitor. The screen also gives you information on the time elapsed, calories burned, distanced traveled, your heart rate, and more.&#160;</li><li><strong>Weight limit: </strong>Based on the size of the motor and on the shock absorption capabilities, a treadmill may give you a maximum user weight recommendation.&#160;</li><li><strong>Wi-Fi connection: </strong>Through a Wi-Fi connection, you can gain access to simulated video workouts. Or you can play streaming movies on the display screen, giving you some entertainment as you're workout out on the treadmill.</li><li><strong>Width: </strong>A treadmill belt bed should be at least 22 inches wide for runners which provides plenty of space in case you have a misstep. Walkers can successfully use a narrower bed than runners, such as 18 or 20 inches.</li></ul>\n\tHow we test treadmills\n\t\n\t<p>Each treadmill featured in this guide went through a series of extensive tests (i.e. we ran on them &#8212;&#160;<em>a lot</em>) to see how well they compared across these four categories:&#160;<strong>Performance, features, quality,&#160;</strong>and&#160;<strong>value</strong>. Here's how each category specifically factored into which treadmills ended up making this guide:</p><p><strong>Performance:&#160;</strong>How a treadmill performs comes down to a few basic aspects, including how comfortable it is to run on (and how shock absorbing it is), if it's able to avoid sounding like you're loudly pounding the ground with each step, what its tread feels like underfoot, and how wide the running area is. Though not all treadmills reliably check each of these boxes, a healthy combination of at least three of those often translates to high quality.&#160;</p><p><strong>Features:&#160;</strong>Some modern treadmills, like those from Peloton or ProForm, feature a built-in interactive screen that streams workouts, tracks output metrics, and improves the treadmill's performance. For models that don't have a screen, we looked at how intuitive it was to increase and decrease the treadmill's speed and whether it offered an incline or decline mode. Even those that aren't decked out with the ability to stream workouts are still feature-heavy enough to warrant a spot in your home gym.</p><p><strong>Quality:&#160;</strong>If used often, treadmills can take a consistent beating, mostly due to a runner pounding on it step after step after step. This means the best treadmills should feature a sturdy and durable tread, a high-quality design that won't become compromised even after a full year or more of use, and that feature an interface or series of buttons and dials that can avoid popping off or being unusable.&#160;</p><p><strong>Value:&#160;</strong>The value of a treadmill is less about its sticker price and more so the combination of the three categories above compared to its initial (and sometimes recurring) investment. We factored in everything when selecting treadmills across each featured category and often feel that it's worth it to spend a little more money on a product that's designed to last than to spend less, more often on something inferior.&#160;</p>\n</div><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a href='https://www.businessinsider.com/best-treadmill'>Business class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Joe Biden <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/why-ddhq-and-business-insider-called-the-election-for-biden-2020-11\">won the 2020 presidential race</a> with a victory in Pennsylvania, Insider and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/why-ddhq-and-business-insider-called-the-election-for-biden-2020-11\">Decision Desk HQ projected</a> on November 6.&#160;</li>\n<li>Biden needed 270 Electoral College votes necessary to secure the White House. He is now projected to have won 290 electoral votes.</li>\n<li>Trump was projected winner in North Carolina on November 10 and Alaska on November 11. But their combined 18 electoral votes still leave him far short of Biden's total.</li>\n<li>Biden restored Democratic dominance to the \"blue wall\" states of Michigan, Pennsylvania, and Wisconsin that helped President Donald Trump beat former Secretary of State Hillary Clinton in 2016.</li>\n<li>Insider and Decision Desk HQ have not yet projected a winner in only one state, Georgia, where officials are conducting a hand recount of the presidential race.&#160;</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><bi-shortcode id=\"table-of-contents-sticky\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-type=\"h2\">Table of Contents: Masthead Sticky</bi-shortcode><p>President-elect <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/joe-biden-wins-general-election-against-donald-trump-2020-11\">Joe Biden won Pennsylvania's 20 electoral votes</a> and the United States presidency, Insider and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/why-ddhq-and-business-insider-called-the-election-for-biden-2020-11\">Decision Desk HQ projected early November 6.</a></p><p>One day later, Decision Desk HQ projected that Biden would win Nevada's six electoral votes, and projected on November 11 that Biden will win Arizona's 11 Electoral College votes.&#160;</p><p>On November 10, the service projected President Donald Trump would win North Carolina's 15 electoral votes, and on November 11 projected that he would pick up three more votes from Alaska.</p><p>Biden is currently projected to have picked up 290 electoral votes, which puts him far past the 270-vote threshold necessary to unseat Trump, whose total as of Wednesday morning was 232 votes.</p><p>The former vice president also won in the battleground states of Michigan and Wisconsin, restoring Democratic dominance to the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/biden-rebuilding-blue-wall-in-race-for-the-white-house-2020-11\">\"blue wall\" states</a> that helped deliver President Barack Obama's victories in 2008 and 2012.</p><p>Decision Desk HQ has also yet to declare the winner in Georgia, where election officials are conducting a hand recount of the presidential race.</p><p>Biden, who spent the early part of his childhood in Scranton, Pennsylvania, achieved a major priority for Democrats in 2020 by winning back the crucial state. In 2016, Trump <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/elections/2016/results/president\">carried the state by about 44,000 votes</a>, a margin of less than 1 percentage point, to beat former Secretary of State Hillary Clinton.</p><p>This year, Democrats focused on running up the score in the suburban counties around Philadelphia, Harrisburg, and Pittsburgh. They also went toe-to-toe with Trump among the rural and non-college-educated voters they struggled to win in 2016.</p><p>Before Trump, a Republican presidential nominee had not won Pennsylvania since George H.W. Bush narrowly secured the state in 1988.</p><p>While Trump led the vote count on election night, his lead significantly narrowed throughout last week as mail ballots pushed Biden over the top.</p><h3><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/why-ddhq-and-business-insider-called-the-election-for-biden-2020-11\"><em><strong>Read more: </strong>Why DDHQ and Insider called the election for Joe Biden</em></a></h3><section></section><p>The shift in the vote count as mail-in ballots were processed was particularly dramatic for two main reasons. First, Trump spent much of the pandemic denigrating voting by mail and falsely claiming that it is fraudulent and corrupt. This helped to create a sharp partisan division in how Americans cast their ballots.</p><p>Second, Pennsylvania's legislature for the first time this year allowed all residents to vote by mail without an excuse. However, unlike in other swing states, it <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/election-results-may-take-longer-in-michigan-pennsylvania-wisconsin-2020-10\">did not authorize election officials to begin processing or counting mail ballots</a> before the polls opened on Election Day. That meant that while Trump led in the votes reported from in-person Election Day voting, Biden caught up to and then overtook the president as Democratic-leaning mail ballots were processed.</p><p>While Trump is projected to lose the presidency, Decision Desk HQ projected that he would win the battleground states of Florida, Iowa, Ohio, and Texas, as well as Maine's 2nd Congressional District.</p><p>Biden was projected to win Minnesota, Michigan, Wisconsin, and Nebraska's 2nd Congressional District.</p><p>Meanwhile, Trump has repeatedly demanded that vote counting be stopped.</p><p>On November 7, the Trump campaign <a href=\"https://twitter.com/PhilipWegmann/status/1324045073613492224\">said it would demand a recount in Wisconsin</a> — decrying, without evidence, \"irregularities\" in counting for the \"razor thin race\" there. It can file for the recount, however, only after the race is certified later on.</p><p>The Trump campaign also lost several last-minute court challenges in Pennsylvania, Michigan, and Georgia, which were aimed at slowing down or temporarily halting ballot counts.</p><p>As of 10 p.m. on Wednesday, November 11, this was the situation in the states still to call:</p><ul><li><strong>Georgia, 16 electoral votes: </strong>Biden overturned Trump's lead in Georgia on Friday, November 6, as more mail votes were tabulated and reported in the Democratic-leaning counties around Atlanta. Biden is now ahead by some 14,000 votes.<ul><li>Secretary of State Brad Raffensperger <a href=\"https://www.gpb.org/events/news/2020/11/11/secretary-of-states-office-addresses-georgia-election-results\">announced on Wednesday, November 11</a>, that the state will conduct a combination of a risk-limiting audit, re-canvass, and hand recount of the presidential race between Biden and Trump to be completed by the state's certification deadline on November 20.&#160;</li></ul></li></ul><p>In addition to the presidential race, hundreds of critical Senate and House races on the ballot this fall will determine the balance of power in Washington, DC, for years to come.</p><p>Before the election, some analysts said that based on polling and fundraising data before the election, Democrats were <a href=\"https://cookpolitical.com/analysis/senate/senate-overview/final-2020-senate-overview-democrats-remain-favorites-take-senate\">favored to win back the Senate</a> and <a href=\"https://cookpolitical.com/analysis/house/house-overview/final-house-ratings-democrats-poised-expand-majority-10-15-seats\">grow their majority in the House.</a> But so far, the Democrats are having a disappointing week.</p><p>With losses in Maine, Iowa, Montana, and Kansas, Democrats have a narrow path to retaking control of the Senate. They flipped Senate seats in Colorado and Arizona but would need to win <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/georgia-senate-runoff-elections-jon-ossoff-david-perdue-warnock-loeffler-2020-11\">both runoff Senate elections in Georgia in January</a> to get to a 50-50 tie with Republicans.</p><p>And in the House, Democrats are likely to see the size of their majority shrink rather than expand.</p><h3>See Insider's full coverage of <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/2020-senate-election-results\">the race for the US Senate</a>, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/2020-house-elections-results\">the US House elections</a>, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/guide-to-2020-gubernatorial-elections-explainers-live-results-2020-11\">2020's gubernatorial elections</a>, and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/guide-to-key-ballot-initiatives-propositions-in-2020-results-2020-11\">some of the most critical ballot initiatives</a> around the country.</h3><h2>The swing states we were watching</h2><p>Here's what you need to know about the top 10 swing states and how analysts predicted they would turn out:</p><p>Six states — Florida, Iowa, Michigan, Ohio, Pennsylvania, Wisconsin — flipped from voting for President Barack Obama in 2012 to voting for Trump in 2016.</p><ul><li><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/arizona-presidential-election-2020-live-vote-counts-results-2020\">Arizona</a>, </strong>which Decision Desk HQ projects for Biden,&#160;accounts for 11 votes in the Electoral College.<ul><li>In 2016, Trump carried the state <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/elections/2016/results/president\">by a margin of 3.5 points</a> over the Democratic nominee, Hillary Clinton. In FiveThirtyEight's <a href=\"https://projects.fivethirtyeight.com/polls/president-general/arizona/\">final average of 2020 general-election polls in Arizona</a>, Biden led Trump by 2.6 points.</li></ul></li><li><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/florida-presidential-election-2020-live-vote-counts-results-2020\">Florida</a></strong>, which Decision Desk HQ projects for Trump, accounts for 29 votes in the Electoral College.<ul><li>In 2016, Trump carried the state by <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/elections/2016/results/president\">a margin of 1.2 points</a> over Clinton. In FiveThirtyEight's <a href=\"https://projects.fivethirtyeight.com/polls/president-general/florida/\">final average of 2020 polls in Florida</a>, Biden led Trump by 2.5 points.</li></ul></li><li><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/georgia-presidential-election-2020-live-vote-counts-results-2020\">Georgia</a></strong> accounts for 16 votes in the Electoral College.<ul><li>In 2016, Trump won Georgia <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/elections/2016/results/president\">by a margin of 5.1 points</a> over Clinton. In FiveThirtyEight's <a href=\"https://projects.fivethirtyeight.com/polls/president-general/georgia/\">average of 2020 polls in Georgia</a>, Biden led Trump by 1.2 points.</li></ul></li><li><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/iowa-presidential-election-2020-live-vote-counts-results-2020\">Iowa</a></strong>, which Decision Desk HQ projects for Trump, accounts for six votes in the Electoral College.<ul><li>In 2016, Trump won Iowa by a margin of 9.4 points over Clinton. In FiveThirtyEight's <a href=\"https://projects.fivethirtyeight.com/polls/president-general/iowa/\">average of 2020 polls in Iowa</a>, Trump led Biden by 1.3 points.</li></ul></li><li><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/michigan-presidential-election-2020-live-vote-counts-results-2020\">Michigan</a></strong>, which Decision Desk HQ projects for Biden, accounts for 16 votes in the Electoral College.<ul><li>In 2016, Trump carried Michigan by a margin of 0.3 points over Clinton. In FiveThirtyEight's <a href=\"https://projects.fivethirtyeight.com/polls/president-general/michigan/\">average of 2020 general-election polls in Michigan</a>, Biden led Trump by 7.9 points.<a href=\"https://insideelections.com/ratings/president\"></a></li></ul></li><li><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/north-carolina-presidential-election-2020-live-vote-counts-results-2020\">North Carolina</a></strong>, which Decision Desk HQ projects for Trump, accounts for 15 votes in the Electoral College.<ul><li>In 2016, Trump carried North Carolina by a margin of 3.6 points over Clinton. In FiveThirtyEight's <a href=\"https://projects.fivethirtyeight.com/polls/president-general/north-carolina/\">average of 2020 general-election polls in North Carolina</a>, Biden led Trump by 1.8 points.</li></ul></li><li><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/ohio-presidential-election-2020-live-vote-counts-results-2020\">Ohio</a></strong>, which Decision Desk HQ projects for Trump, accounts for 18 Electoral College votes.<ul><li>In 2016, Trump carried Ohio by a margin of 8.1 points over Clinton. In FiveThirtyEight's <a href=\"https://projects.fivethirtyeight.com/polls/president-general/ohio/\">average of 2020 general-election polls in Ohio</a>, Trump led Biden by 0.8 points.</li></ul></li><li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/pennsylvania-presidential-election-2020-live-vote-counts-results-2020\"><strong>Pennsylvania</strong></a>,&#160;which Decision Desk HQ projects for Biden, accounts for 20 electoral votes.<ul><li>In 2016, Trump carried Pennsylvania by a margin of 0.7 points over Clinton. In FiveThirtyEight's <a href=\"https://projects.fivethirtyeight.com/polls/president-general/pennsylvania/\">average of 2020 general-election polls in Pennsylvania</a>, Biden led Trump by 4.7 points.</li></ul></li><li><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/texas-presidential-election-2020-live-vote-counts-results-2020\">Texas</a></strong>, which Decision Desk HQ projects for Trump, accounts for 38 electoral votes.<ul><li>In 2016, Trump carried Texas by a margin of 9 points over Clinton. In FiveThirtyEight's <a href=\"https://projects.fivethirtyeight.com/polls/president-general/texas/\">average of 2020 general-election polls in Texas</a>, Trump led Biden by 1.1 points.</li></ul></li><li><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/wisconsin-presidential-election-2020-live-vote-counts-results-2020\">Wisconsin</a></strong>, which Decision Desk HQ projects for Biden, accounts for 10 electoral votes.<ul><li>In 2016, Trump carried Wisconsin by a margin of 0.7 points over Clinton. In FiveThirtyEight's <a href=\"https://projects.fivethirtyeight.com/polls/president-general/wisconsin/\">average of 2020 general-election polls</a>, Biden led Trump by 8.4
